Iinkonzo zoluntu 
Isixeko saseLondon idyasi yengalo esitratweni 
AmaPolisa nokhuseleko 
Ulwazi oluthe vetshe: Ulwaphulo-mthetho eLondon

 
Isithuthi samaPolisa eSixeko saseLondon eBlackfriars Bridge
Isixeko siyindawo yamapolisa kwaye sinamapolisa aso, isiXeko samaPolisa aseLondon, esahlukileyo kwiNkonzo yamaPolisa eMetropolitan ethatha uninzi lweLondon enkulu. AmaPolisa eSixeko ngaphambili ayenezikhululo zamapolisa ezithathu, eSnow Hill, eWood Street naseBishopsgate. Ngoku bagcina iBishopsgate kunye nekomkhulu lolawulo eGuildhall Yard East.[57] Umkhosi ubandakanya amagosa asebupoliseni angama-735 kuquka nabacuphi abangama-273. [58] Ngowona mkhosi umncinci wamapolisa eNgilane naseWales, kuzo zombini iindawo zejografi kunye nenani lamapolisa. 

Apho uninzi lwamapolisa ase-Bhritane aneebheji ezinemibala yesilivere, ezo zamaPolisa eSixeko saseLondon zimnyama kunye negolide ezineCity of City. Umkhosi unamabhendi e-cap ye-checkered ebomvu namhlophe kunye nebhanti yengalo ekhethekileyo ebomvu nemhlophe enemigca emhlophe kwimikhono yeengubo zooconstable kunye neesejini (imibala ebomvu nemhlophe yimibala yesixeko), apho uninzi lwamapolisa aseBritane amnyama namhlophe. Amapolisa esixeko kunye nooConstable banxiba izigcina-ntloko ezigciniweyo ngelixa behamba ngeenyawo. Ezi helmethi azibonisi nokuba yiSt Edward's Crown okanye iBrunswick Star, ezisetyenziswa kwezinye izigcina-ntloko zamapolisa eNgilani naseWales. 

Isikhundla sesixeko njengeziko lezemali lase-United Kingdom kunye nenxalenye ebalulekileyo yoqoqosho lwelizwe, igalelo malunga ne-2.5% yemveliso yesizwe yase-UK, [59] ibangele ukuba ibe yinto ekujoliswe kuyo kubundlobongela bezopolitiko. I-IRA yoBonelelo yaqhuma iibhombu ezininzi ekuqaleni kweminyaka yoo-1990, kubandakanywa nebhombu ye-Bishopsgate ka-1993. 

Lo mmandla ukwathethwa ngawo njengendawo ekujoliswe kuyo i-al-Qaeda. Ngokomzekelo, xa ngoMeyi 2004 inkqubo yeBBC iPanorama yavavanya ukulungela kweenkonzo zikaxakeka zaseBritani kuhlaselo lwabanqolobi ngomhla we-11 kuSeptemba 2001, balinganisa ugqabhuko lwemichiza eBishopsgate kwimpuma yesixeko. I-"Ring of Steel" yasekwa emva koqhushumbo lwe-IRA ukugada izoyikiso zabanqolobi. 

I-Fire brigade 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-London Fire Brigade 
Isixeko sinomngcipheko womlilo kwizakhiwo ezininzi zembali, kuquka i-St Paul's Cathedral, i-Old Bailey, i-Mansion House, i-Smithfield Market, i-Guildhall, kunye nezakhiwo ezininzi eziphakamileyo. Kukho isikhululo saseLondon Fire Brigade esixekweni, eDowgate, kunye nesixhobo sokumpompa esinye. [60] IsiXeko sithembele kwizikhululo ezikwiindawo ezingqonge iLondon ukuba zisixhase kwezinye iziganeko. Isixhobo somlilo sokuqala sihamba malunga nemizuzu emihlanu ngokomndilili, eyesibini xa sifuneka kwisithuba esingaphezu kwemizuzu emihlanu enesiqingatha.[60] Kweza iziganeko ezili-1 814 kwisiXeko ngowama-2006/2007—esona siganeko siphantsi kwiGreater London. Akukho mntu uswelekileyo kwisiganeko esibangelwe kumlilo kwiminyaka emine ephambi kwaloo ndawo 

Amandla 
Kukho isikhululo sombane esiseCharterhouse Street ekwabonelela ngobushushu kwezinye zezakhiwo ezingqongileyo.[61]

Imithombo: I-Ofisi yeeNkcukacha-manani zeSizwe[62][63] 
I-Ofisi yeeNkcukacha-manani zeSizwe irekhode inani labemi ngo-2011 njenge-7,375;[64] ingaphezulu kancinane kunobalo lwabantu lwangaphambili, ngo-2001,[65] kwaye iqikelela ukuba inani labemi phakathi ku-2016 libe ngama-9,401. Kubalo-bantu luka-2001 ukwakheka kobuhlanga bekungama-84.6% abaMhlophe, 6.8% abaMnyama baseAsia, 2.6% abaMnyama, 2.3% abaxubileyo, 2.0% amaTshayina kunye ne-1.7% zidweliswe "njengabanye".[65] Inani labemi beliphakathi kwe-120,000 kunye ne-140,000 kwisiqingatha sokuqala senkulungwane ye-19, lehla ngokumangalisayo ukusuka ku-1851 ukuya ku-1991, kunye nokwanda okuncinci phakathi kuka-1991 no-2001. Olona tshintsho lwemida oluqaphelekayo ukusukela kubalo lwabantu lokuqala ngo-1801 lwenzeka 

kwidolophu esebenza ngokuzeleyo ngeveki ka -1994. hlawula kunaseLondon naseGreat Britain (eNgilani, eWales naseSkotlani): £773.30 xa kuthelekiswa ne-£598.60 kunye ne-£491.00 ngokulandelelanayo [66] Kukho ukungalingani okukhulu kwengeniso phakathi kwamadoda (i-£ 1,085.90 kumadoda xa kuthelekiswa ne-£ 653.50 kwabasetyhini), kwaye oku kunokuchazwa ngohlobo lomsebenzi kunye nobude bengqesho ngokulandelelanayo.[66] UBalo luka-2001 lubonise isixeko njengesithili esisodwa phakathi kwezithili ezingama-376 eziphononongwe eNgilani naseWales. [65] Esi sixeko sasinolona lwando luphezulu lwabemi ngokomlinganiselo, amakhaya anomntu omnye, abantu abaneziqinisekiso zemfundo kwinqanaba lesidanga okanye ngaphezulu kunye nezalathi eziphezulu zokuxinana.[65] Irekhode eyona nxalenye iphantsi yemizi eneemoto okanye iiveni, abantu abahamba ukuya emsebenzini ngemoto, amakhaya abantu abatshatileyo kunye nowona mlinganiselo uphantsi wobukhulu bendlu: abantu abayi-1.58 kuphela.[65] Ikwabeka kwindawo ephezulu phakathi kweNgingqi yaseLondon enkulu kwipesenti yabantu abangenayo inkolo kunye nabantu abasebenzayo.[65] 

Ukuwohloka kwamanani abantu kwiSixeko saseLondon (1981-2021) 
Uqoqosho 
Bona kwakhona: UQoqosho lwaseLondon
 
IBhanki yaseNgilani, kwiSitalato iThreadneedle, yibhanki ephakathi yaseUnited Kingdom.
IsiXeko saseLondon sikhuphisana neNew York City yaseLower Manhattan ukohlula iziko lezemali elibalaseleyo kwihlabathi. ILondon Stock Exchange (izabelo kunye neebhondi), uLloyd's waseLondon (i-inshurensi) kunye neBhanki yaseNgilani zonke zizinze esixekweni.[72] Iibhanki ezingaphezu kwama-500 zineeofisi esixekweni. I-Alternative Investment Market, imarike yorhwebo kwi-equities yeefemu ezincinci, luphuhliso lwakutsha nje. Ngo-2009, isiXeko saseLondon sasibalelwa kwi-2.4% yeGDP yase-UK.[73] 

Imarike yotshintshiselwano lwangaphandle yaseLondon ichazwe yiReuters njenge 'jewel yesithsaba secandelo lezemali laseLondon'. [74] Kwi-3.98 yezigidi zezigidi zezigidi zeedola emhlabeni jikelele, njengoko kulinganiswe ngo-2009, urhwebo eLondon lubalele malunga ne-1.85 yezigidigidi zeedola, okanye i-46.7% yetotali. [73] Ipound sterling, imali yase-United Kingdom, yimali yesine ekurhwetywa ngayo kwihlabathi jikelele [75] kunye neyesine eyona mali yogcino igcinwe.[76] 

ICanary Wharf, iimayile ezimbalwa kwimpuma yeSixeko eTower Hamlets, enemizi yeebhanki ezininzi kunye namanye amaziko ebefudula ekwiSquare Mile, ukusukela ngo-1991 iye yaba lelinye iziko loshishino lweenkonzo zemali eLondon. Nangona ukukhula kuqhubekile kuzo zombini iindawo, [kungacacanga] kwaye kuye kwakho ukufuduswa macala omabini, iQumrhu liye laqonda ukuba imigaqo-nkqubo yalo yokucwangcisa isenokuba ibibangela ukuba iifemu zezemali zikhethe iCanary Wharf njengendawo 

. 

Headquarters 

Paternoster Square, ukususela 2004 ikhaya London Stock Exchange 
Iinkampani ezininzi ezinkulu zehlabathi ikomkhulu labo kwisixeko, kuquka Aviva, [78] BT Group, [79] Lloyds Banking Group, [80] Quilter, Prudential, [81] Schroders, [82] Standard Chartered, [83] kunye Unilever, [83] [83] 

Uninzi lweefemu ezinkulu zezomthetho zehlabathi zikomkhulu kwisixeko, kubandakanya ezine zeefemu zomthetho zeSangqa seMagic (Allen & Overy, Freshfields Bruckhaus Deringer, Linklaters and Slaughter & May), kunye nezinye iifemu ezifana neAshurst, DLA Piper, Eversheds Sutherland, Herbert Smith Freehills. 

Amanye amacandelo 

Barbican Centre
Ngelixa icandelo lezemali, kunye namashishini anxulumeneyo kunye namaziko, eqhubeleka elawula, uqoqosho aluphelelanga kwelo candelo. Ubuchwephesha bezomthetho bunobukho obunamandla, ngakumbi entshona nangasentla (oko kukuthi, ngakwiNdawo yokulala yeNkundla). Amashishini okuthengisa ayekhe abalulekile, kodwa ngokuthe ngcembe afudukela kwi-West End yaseLondon, nangona ngoku ingumgaqo-nkqubo we-Corporation ukukhuthaza ukuthengiswa kwezinye iindawo, umzekelo e-Cheapside kufuphi ne-St Paul's. Isixeko sinenani leendawo ezinomtsalane kubakhenkethi, ikakhulu ngokusekwe kwimbali yaso yelifa kunye neZiko leBarbican kunye neMyuziyam ekufutshane yaseLondon, nangona ukhenketho okwangoku alulogalelo liphambili kuqoqosho lwesixeko okanye umlinganiswa. Isixeko sinee-pubs ezininzi, imivalo kunye neendawo zokutyela, kwaye uqoqosho "lwexesha lasebusuku" lubonakala kwindawo yaseBishopsgate, ukuya ngaseShoreditch. Imakethi yenyama eSmithfield, ngaphakathi esixekweni, isaqhubeka iyenye yeemarike eziphambili zaseLondon (ekuphela kwayo eseleyo kumbindi weLondon) kunye neyona marike inkulu yelizwe. Empuma kukho iMarike yaseLeadenhall, imarike yokutya okutsha ekwanomtsalane kubakhenkethi. 

Ukuthengisa kunye neendawo zokuhlala 
Intsingiselo yophuhliso lwee-ofisi kuphela iqalisa ukubuya umva njengoko iQumrhu likhuthaza usetyenziso lweendawo zokuhlala, nangona uphuhliso lwenzeka xa luvela kwiziza zomoya. Esi sixeko sijolise ekubeni neendawo zokuhlala ezongezelelweyo ezingama-90 ngonyaka.[85] Enye indawo yokuhlala eyongezelelekileyo ikwizakhiwo ezincinci ezidweliswe ngaphambi kweMfazwe Yehlabathi II, ezingakulungelanga ukuhlalwa ziinkampani ezinkulu ezibonelela ngokuqeshwa kwabantu abaninzi kwesi sixeko. Uphuhliso lwakutsha nje lwendawo yokuhlala lubandakanya "iHeron", isakhiwo esiphakamileyo sokuhlala kwindawo yaseMilton Court ekufuphi neBarbican, kunye nophuhliso lweHeron Plaza eBishopsgate kulindeleke ukuba luquke iindawo zokuhlala. 

Ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-1990, isiXeko siye sahlukana sisuka ekusetyenzisweni kwee-ofisi ezikufutshane ngezinye iindlela. Umzekelo, iihotele ezininzi kunye nevenkile yokuqala yavulwa ngeminyaka yoo-2000. Indawo yeevenkile isanda kuvulwa eOne New Change, eCheapside (kufuphi neSt Paul's Cathedral) ngo-Okthobha ka-2010, evula iintsuku ezisixhenxe ngeveki. Nangona kunjalo, amacandelo amakhulu ahlala ethe cwaka ngeempelaveki, ngakumbi kwicandelo lasempuma, kwaye kuyinto eqhelekileyo ukufumana iivenkile, ii-pubs kunye neecafe zivaliwe kwezi ntsuku. 

Amanqaku omhlaba 
Izakhiwo zembali 
Umlilo, ukuqhushumbiswa kwebhombu kunye nophuhliso lwasemva kweMfazwe yesibini yeHlabathi kuthethe ukuba isixeko, ngaphandle kwembali yaso, sinezakhiwo ezimbalwa zembali ezingaguqukiyo kunokuba umntu ebenokulindela. Nangona kunjalo, kusekho intaphane yezakhiwo ezintle (ubukhulu becala iVictorian kunye ne-Edwardian), ngokwesiqhelo kwimbali kunye nesimbo se-neoclassical. Ziquka iSikhumbuzo soMlilo oMkhulu waseLondon ("iSikhumbuzo"), iSt Paul's Cathedral, iGuildhall, iRoyal Exchange, iNdlu kaDkt Johnson, i-Mansion House kunye neecawa ezininzi, ezininzi ziyilwe nguSir Christopher Wren, owayila iSt.

Igumbi leNkosana uHenry kunye ne-2 King's Bench Walk ngamaxhoba aphawulekayo kwimbali yokuqhushumba kwebhombu kwindawo yeTempile, ethe yaphinda yakhiwa ngokutsha ngokwembali yayo. Omnye umzekelo wendawo eyonakaliswe yibhombu ebuyiselweyo yiStaple Inn eHolborn. Amacandelo amancinci ambalwa oDonga lwaseLondon lwaseRoma lukhona, umzekelo kufuphi neNqaba yaseLondon kunye nommandla weBarbican. Phakathi kwezakhiwo ezidwelisiweyo zenkulungwane yamashumi amabini kukho iBracken House, izakhiwo zokuqala emva kweMfazwe yeHlabathi yesiBini elizweni ezinikwe ukhuseleko olusemthethweni, kunye neBarbican yonke kunye neGolden Lane Estate. 

INqaba yaseLondon ayikho esixekweni, kodwa iyindawo enomtsalane kubakhenkethi ezisa abakhenkethi kumazantsi-mpuma esixeko. Ezinye izakhiwo eziphawulekayo ezinokubaluleka kwembali ziquka iBhanki yaseNgilani, i-Old Bailey, i-Custom House, iMarike yaseSmithfield, iMarike yaseLeadenhall kunye neSibhedlele saseSt Bartholomew. Izakhiwo eziphawulekayo zala maxesha ziquka intlaninge yezakhiwo zale mihla eziphakamileyo (bona icandelo elingezantsi) kunye nesakhiwo sikaLloyd. 


IBhanki yaseNgilani (ekhohlo) kunye neRoyal Exchange (embindini) zizakhiwo ezininzi ezibalulekileyo kwiSixeko saseLondon. 
Izakhiwo eziphakamileyo kunye nezakhiwo ezide 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lwezona zakhiwo zide kunye nezakhiwo eLondon 

Isibhakabhaka seSixeko ngo-2021, kubandakanywa ne-20 Fenchurch Street, iSakhiwo saseLeadenhall, 30 St Mary Ax & 22 Bishopgate, esona sakhiwo side kwiSixeko saseLondon. London Bridge ukuya emazantsi ekhohlo. 
Kugqitywe 
Inani elikhulayo lezakhiwo ezide kunye nezakhiwo eziphakamileyo ezisetyenziswa ikakhulu licandelo lezemali. Phantse zonke zime kwicala elingasempuma elijikeleze iBishopsgate, iLeadenhall Street kunye neFenchurch Street, kumbindi wemali wesixeko. Emantla kukho iqela elincinane elibandakanya iBarbican Estate's ezintathu iinqaba zokuhlala ezinde kunye neyona ndawo ithengisayo yeCityPoint. Ngo-2007, i-100 m (328 ft) isakhiwo se-Drapers' Gardens esinde sadilizwa kwaze kwafakwa inqaba emfutshane. 

Izakhiwo zesixeko ezinobuncinci be-100 m (328 ft) ubude zezi: 



UJames Gillray (13 Agasti 1756 [1][2] - 1 Juni 1815) wayeyi-caricaturist yaseBritane kunye nomshicileli odumileyo ngenxa yokuhlekisa kwakhe kwezopolitiko kunye nentlalontle, epapashwe phakathi kwe-1792 kunye ne-1810. 

UGillray ubizwa ngokuba "nguyise wekhathuni yezopolitiko", kunye nemisebenzi yakhe ehlekisa uGeorge III, uNapoleon, iinkulumbuso kunye neenjengele. Ethathwa njengomnye wabona bakhathuni banempembelelo enkulu, omnye inguWilliam Hogarth, ubukrelekrele noburharha bukaGillray, ulwazi lobomi, ukuchuma kobutyebi, ukuqonda okubukhali, kunye nobuhle bokubulawa, kwangoko wamnika indawo yokuqala phakathi kwabadlali becaricaturists. [3] [4] [5]
 
Obomi bakwangoko
Wazalelwa e-Chelsea, eLondon. Uyise wayelijoni; waphulukana nengalo kwiDabi laseFontenoy ngo-1745 waza wamkelwa, okokuqala njengebanjwa waza emva koko wangumntu odla umhlala-phantsi, kwiSibhedlele sase-Chelsea. UGillray waqalisa ubomi ngokufunda ukubhala ngoonobumba, apho waba nobuchule khona. Ukufumana lo msebenzi udinisayo, emva koko wabhadula kangangexesha elithile kunye nenkampani yabadlali abahambahambayo. Emva kwamava checkered, wabuyela eLondon waza wamkelwa njengomfundi kwiRoyal Academy, ezixhasa ngokukrola, yaye mhlawumbi ekhupha inani elikhulu caricatures phantsi kwamagama obuxoki.[6] 

I-caricatures yakhe phantse yonke ikwi-etching, abanye bane-aquatint, kwaye abambalwa basebenzisa ubuchule be-stipple. Akukho nanye inokuchazwa ngokuchanekileyo njengemizobo, nangona eli gama lidla ngokusetyenziswa ngokukhululekileyo ukuyichaza. Imisebenzi kaHogarth yayiluyolo kunye nesifundo seminyaka yakhe yokuqala. I-Paddy kwi-Horseback, eyavela ngo-1779, yi-caricature yokuqala ngokuqinisekileyo yeyakhe. Imifanekiso eshukumayo emibini yoloyiso lwaselwandle lukaAdmiral Rodney kwiDabi laseSaintes, elakhutshwa ngo-1782, yayiphakathi kwezokuqala kuthotho olukhumbulekayo lwemizobo yakhe yezopolitiko. [6][7] 

Ubomi bomntu omdala 

Very Slippy-Weather (1808) 
Igama lompapashi nomthengisi woshicilelo kaGillray, uHannah Humphrey – ovenkile yakhe yaqala e-227 Strand, emva koko yaseNew Bond Street, yaza yaya kwisitalato i-Old Bond, yaza ekugqibeleni yaya kwisitalato i-St James’s – linxulunyaniswa ngokungenakuhlukaniswa nelo lecaricaturist ngokwakhe. UGillray wayehlala noMiss (odla ngokuba nguNksk) uHumphrey ngalo lonke ixesha lodumo lwakhe. Kukholelwa ukuba izihlandlo ezininzi wayecinga ngokutshata naye, yaye ngesinye isihlandlo esi sibini sasisendleleni eya ecaweni, xa uGillray wathi: “Lo ngumcimbi wobudenge, ucinga, uNkosazana Humphrey. Akukho bungqina, nangona kunjalo, ukuxhasa amabali aqanjwa ngabadlali behlazo malunga nobudlelwane babo.[6] Olunye lweempapasho zikaGillray, "Twopenny Whist", ngumfanekiso wabantu abane abadlala amakhadi, kwaye umlinganiswa oboniswe wesibini ukusuka ekhohlo, inenekazi esele likhulile elineendondo zamehlo kunye nebhonethi, kukholelwa ngokubanzi ukuba ngumfanekiso ochanekileyo kaMiss Humphrey. 

Iipleyiti zikaGillray zavezwa kwifestile yevenkile kaHumphrey, apho izihlwele ezilangazelelayo zawahlola.[6] Enye yeempapasho zakhe zamva, i- Very Slippy-Weather, ibonisa ivenkile ka-Miss Humphrey e-St. James's Street ngasemva. Kwifestile yevenkile inani leeprinta ezipapashwe ngaphambili zikaGillray, ezifana noTiddy-Doll uMenzi we-Gingerbread omkhulu waseFransi, Ukukhupha iBatch entsha yeeKumkani; Indoda Yakhe, Talley Mixing up the Dough, satire on Napoleon's proclivities-making proclivities, iboniswe kwifestile yevenkile. 


I-L'Assemblée Nationale (1804) yayibizwa ngokuba "yeyona caricature inetalente yakha yavela", ngokuyinxenye ngenxa "yemifanekiselo encomekayo".INkosana yaseWales yahlawula intywenka yemali ukuze icinezelwe ize ipleyiti yayo itshatyalaliswe.[8]
Amehlo kaGillray aqala ukungaboni kakuhle ngowe-1806. Engakwazi ukusebenza kwimilinganiselo yakhe ephakamileyo yangaphambili, uJames Gillray wadandatheka waza waqalisa ukusela kakhulu. Wavelisa ushicilelo lwakhe lokugqibela ngoSeptemba 1809. Ngenxa yokusela kwakhe kakhulu uGillray wahlaselwa yigawuthi kubo bonke ubomi bakhe bamva. 

Umsebenzi wakhe wokugqibela, ovela kuyilo nguBunbury, unesihloko esithi Interior of a Barber's Shop in Assize Time, kwaye yabhalwa ngo-1811. Ngelixa wayezibandakanya kuyo waphambana, nangona wayenamathuba athile engqondo, awayiqasha kumsebenzi wakhe wokugqibela. Impambano isenokuba yayikhawuleziswa yimikhwa yakhe yokungabi nasimilo.[6] 

NgoJulayi 1811 uGillray wazama ukuzibulala ngokutsiba kwifestile ye-attic ngaphezulu kwevenkile kaHumphrey eSt James's Street. UGillray waphelelwa yimpambano waza wajongwa nguHannah Humphrey de wafa ngomhla woku-1 kuJuni ngo-1815 eLondon; wangcwatyelwa eSt James's churchyard, ePiccadilly. 

Ubugcisa be-caricature 

Ukwamkelwa kweDiplomatique (i-Macartney) kunye ne-Suite yakhe, kwiNkundla yasePekin, epapashwe ngoSeptemba 1792. 
Inani leengqungquthela zakhe ezithintekayo zijoliswe kuGeorge III, owathi, emva kokuhlola ezinye zeemifanekiso zeGillray, wathi "Andiyiqondi le mifanekiso." UGillray waziphindezela ngenxa yale ntetho yi-caricature yakhe enesihloko esithi A Connoisseur Uvavanya i-Cooper, ayenzayo ngokusebenzisa ikhandlela kwi-"save-all", ukuze i-sketch satirises kwangoko i-pretensions yokumkani yolwazi lobugcisa kunye nemikhwa yakhe yobugqwirha.[6] 

Ngexesha leNguqulelo yesiFrentshi, uGillray wathatha isimo sokuzimela, kwaye wakhupha i-caricature emva kwecaricature egculela amaFrentshi kunye neNapoleon (ehlala esebenzisa uJacobin) kwaye ezukisa uJohn Bull. Uninzi lwezi lwapapashwa kwiAnti-Jacobin Review. Nangona kunjalo, akufuneki acingelwe njengomntu onomdla wezopolitiko we-Whig okanye iqela le-Tory; iicaricatures zakhe zanelise amalungu awo onke amacala ezopolitiko.[6] 


IiCraws eziMonstrous, kuMthendeleko oMtsha woManyano (1787)
Amaxesha awayephila ngawo uGillray ayethandeka ngokukodwa ekukhuleni kwesikolo esikhulu secaricature. Umlo weqela wawuqhutywa ngamandla amakhulu kwaye hayi kancinci kancinci; kwaye ubuntu babonakaliswa ngokukhululekileyo kumacala omabini. Ubukrelekrele noburharha obungenakuthelekiswa nanto bukaGillray, ulwazi lobomi, ukuchuma kobutyebi, ukuqonda okubukhali, kunye nobuhle bokubulawa, ngoko nangoko kwamnika indawo yokuqala phakathi kwabadlali becaricaturists. Uhluke kwimbali ye-caricature ngento yokuba imizobo yakhe yimisebenzi yokwenene yobugcisa. Iingcamango eziqulethwe kwezinye zazo ziqaqambile yaye ziqaqambile ngokwembongo ngenxa yobunzulu bentsingiselo yazo, ngoxa ukungafihlisi—abaye abanye bakubiza ngokuthi buburhabaxa—obubonakaliswa ngabanye kuluphawu lwenkululeko ngokubanzi yonyango eyayixhaphakile kuwo onke amasebe engqondo ngenkulungwane ye-18. Ixabiso lembali lomsebenzi kaGillray liye laqatshelwa ngabafundi abaninzi abaqondayo bembali. Njengoko kuye kwaphawulwa kakuhle: “INkosi uStanhope iye yajika uGillray ukuba aphendule njengentatheli enyanisekileyo yeentetho, kwakunye nomzobi ocebisayo weziganeko.”[4] 


IVoluuptuary under the Horrors of Digestion (1792) 

Ukuthobeka Ukonwabela Isidlo Esineziqhamo (1792) 
Ingqina lakhe lelo xesha ukuya kwimpembelelo yezobupolitika yomhla we-3 kaNovemba lingqina lezobupolitika eliphuma kwi-3 kaNovemba. 1798. "Abaphikisayo", ubhalela uGillray, "baphantsi njengoko sinokubanqwenelela. Uye waba nenkonzo engapheliyo ekunciphiseni, kwaye ubenze bahlekise." Ishishini elingaqhelekanga likaGillray linokuthi lithathwe kwinto yokuba phantse ii-caricatures ze-1000 ziye zachazwa kuye; ngoxa abanye bemgqala njengombhali weencwadi ezininzi ezisusela kowe-1600 okanye owe-1700. Ngokutsho kwe-Encyclopædia Britannica Eleventh Edition, “uGillray uxabiseke kakhulu kumfundi wesiNgesi njengomfundi wezobupolitika, ehlasela ubutyhakala belo xesha ngokuqhula okuhlazisayo; yaye akukho nto isindayo kwingqalelo yakhe, kwanotshintsho oluncinane oluncinane lwefashoni yefashoni. Nasiphi na isifundo silingana kuphela nokugqitywa okugqibeleleyo kwemizobo yakhe-eyona nto intle ifikelela kubungangamsha obumangalisayo kunye neMiltonic sublimity yokukhawula."[4]

Iicaricatures zikaGillray ngokubanzi zahlulwe zibe ziiklasi ezimbini, uchungechunge lwezopolitiko kunye nentlalontle, nangona kubalulekile ukuba ungabandakanyi igama elithi "uchungechunge" nayiphi na ingcamango yokuqhubeka okanye ukuphelela. Iimpawu zezopolitiko ziquka icandelo elibalulekileyo nelixabiseke kakhulu kwimbali ekhoyo kwinxalenye yokugqibela yolawulo lukaGeorge III. Zazisasazwa kungekuphela nje eBritani kodwa kwanakulo lonke elaseYurophu, yaye zaba nempembelelo enamandla kokubini eBritani nakwamanye amazwe. Kushicilelo lwezopolitiko, uGeorge III, umfazi kaGeorge uKumkanikazi uCharlotte, iNkosana yaseWales (kamva isikhulu senkosi, emva koko uKumkani uGeorge IV), uFox, uPitt oMncinci, uBurke kunye noNapoleon Bonaparte ngabona bantu babalaseleyo. Ngasekupheleni kobomi bakhe, uNapoleon wakhalaza ngelithi imifanekiso eshukumayo kaGillray ethi wayemfutshane ngokungaqhelekanga “yenze ngaphezu kwayo yonke imikhosi yaseYurophu ukundiwisa.”[9] 

Ngowe-1788, kwavela imifanekiso emibini emihle kaGillray. Igazi kwiNdudumo ewela uLwandle oluBomvu imele iNkosi uThurlow ethwele uWarren Hastings kulwandle olushushu: UHastings ubonakala ekhululekile kakhulu, kwaye uphethe iingxowa ezimbini ezinkulu zemali. I-Market-Day ifanekisela abaphathiswa belo xesha njengeenkomo ezithengiswayo.[4] 


KwiFashoni ngaphambi kokukhululeka; – okanye, – UMgaqo-siseko olungileyo wabingelelwa kwiFomu yeFantastick (1793), uJames Gillray wecaricatured Paine eqinisa icorset yaseBritannia kwaye ephuma epokothweni yedyasi yakhe yiteyiphu yokulinganisa ebhalwe "Amalungelo oMntu" 

IPlumb-pudding in Danger (1805). Umhlaba ukrolwe waba ngamacandelo empembelelo phakathi kwePitt kunye neNapoleon. Ngokutsho kukaMartin Rowson, “mhlawumbi yeyona ikhathuni idumileyo kwezobupolitika kulo lonke ixesha, iye yabiwa ngokuphindaphindiweyo ngabazobi ukususela ngoko.” [10] 

I-Cow-Pock—okanye—IziPhumo Ezimangalisayo Zokuchaswa Okutsha! (1802). Iveliswe emva kokuba u-Edward Jenner esebenzise isitofu sokugonya sokuqala, umsebenzi ka-Gillray wabonisa uloyiko lokuba izigulane ziye zagonywa kwingqakaqha nge-cowpox ukuze zihlume izinto ezihlonyelwe njengenkomo. 
Phakathi kwezona satires zibalaseleyo zikaGillray ngoGeorge III zezi: Umlimi uGeorge noMfazi wakhe, iipleyiti ezingamaqabane amabini, kwelinye apho ukumkani ethoja iimuffins kwisidlo sakusasa, aze kwelinye ukumkanikazi aqhotse amaqhekezana; I-Anti-Saccharites, apho isibini sasebukhosini sicebisa ukuba sichithe iswekile, kwintlungu enkulu yentsapho; Ingcali yoVavanyo lweCooper; iipleyiti ezidityanisiweyo A Voluptuary under the Horrors of Digestion and Temperance enjoying a Frugal Meal, satirising excessions of the Prince Regent (kamva uGeorge IV waseUnited Kingdom) kunye nobugwenxa bukayise, uGeorge III waseUnited Kingdom ngokulandelelana; Ukuphatheka kwasebukhosini; Isifundo kwiDumplings yeApile; kunye Neehagu [4]

Ezinye iicaricatures zezopolitiko ziquka: i-Britannia phakathi kwe-Scylla kunye ne-Charybdis, umfanekiso apho u-Pitt, ngokuphindaphindiweyo u-Gillray's butt, ebonisa ukukhanya okulungileyo; Ubusuku boMtshakazi; I-Apotheosis yaseHoche, egxininisa ukugqithiswa kweNguquko yaseFransi kwimbono enye; Indawo egcina abantwana neBritannia ihleli ngoXolo; I-First Kiss kule minyaka ilishumi (1803), enye intlekisa yoxolo, ekuthiwa yamhlekisa kakhulu uNapoleon; Umbhalo wesandla phezu koDonga; I-Confederated Coalition, ukuswayipha kumfelandawonye othathe indawo yobulungiseleli base-Addington; Uncorking Old Sherry; I-Plumb-pudding isengozini (mhlawumbi eyona shicilelo yezopolitiko eyaziwayo eyakha yapapashwa); Ukwenza Isidima; Ukuthuthuzela kwibhedi yeeRozi; Imboniselo yeeHustings eCovent Garden; Phathon Alarmed; kunye noPandora evula iBhokisi yakhe.[4] 

Kanye nokuthetha ngokuphandle ekuqwalaseleni kwakhe, uGillray unokuba nobuqili obumangalisayo, kunye nokubhoboza amampunge ngendlela emangalisayo. Owona mzekelo ubalaseleyo woku lushicilelo lwakhe lweFashion Contrasts;—okanye—I-Duchess's little Shoe yeilding [sic] ukuya kuBukhulu bonyawo lweDuke. Lo yayingumfanekiso owonakalisayo ojolise kwi-sycophancy ehlekisayo eqondiswe ngamajelo eendaba ngokubhekiselele kuFrederica Charlotte Ulrica, iDuchess yaseYork, kunye nokufaneleka kweenyawo zakhe. Ukuprintwa kwabonisa kuphela iinyawo kunye namaqatha eDuke kunye neDuchess yaseYork, kwindawo ecacileyo yokubambisana, kunye neenyawo zeDuke zandiswa kwaye iinyawo zeDuchess zitsalwe zincinci kakhulu. Olu shicilelo lwayithulisa ngonaphakade i-sycophancy ye-press malunga nomanyano lwe-Duke kunye ne-Duchess. 

Uthotho lweentlobo ngeentlobo zeecaricatures, nangona zinqabile ukubaluleka kwembali kuthotho lwezopolitiko, ziqondakala ngokulula, kwaye ziyahlekisa ngakumbi. Phakathi kwezona zibalaseleyo zezi: Shakespeare Sacrificed; IiPenny Whist ezimbini (ezinomfanekiso kaHannah Humphrey); Akwaba le nyama eyomeleleyo inganyibilika; ISandwich-Iminqathe; IGout; Intuthuzelo kwiZikhozo; Begone iNkathalo yobuthuntu; I-Cow-Pock, enika intetho ehlekisayo kuloyiko oludumileyo lokugonywa; Iithiyetha zeDilletanti; kunye neHarmony phambi kweMatrimony and Matrimonial Harmonics-imizobo emibini echasene nobundlobongela enye kwenye.[4] 

I-Flemish Characters (1793), ipapashwe nguG. Humphrey, 27 St James's Street, 1 January 1822

iintlelo ezidumileyo 
Ukhetho lwemisebenzi kaGillray lwavela kuJames Gillray: ICaricatures eprintwe phakathi kwe1818 kunye nembindi ye1820s yaza yapapashwa nguJohn Miller, Bridge Street kunye neW. Blackwood, Edinburgh. Iinxalenye ezisithoba zakhululwa. Uhlelo olulandelayo lwaba lukaThomas McLean, olwapapashwa ngesitshixo ngowe-1830.

Ngowe-1851 uHenry George Bohn wakhupha uhlelo, olusuka kumacwecwe angaphambili kwiphepha lendlovu elibukekayo, elinemizobo erhabaxa—eyaziwa ngokuba “ziPlati Ezicinezelweyo”—elalipapashwa kumqulu owahlukileyo. Kolu hlelo uThomas Wright kunye noRobert Harding Evans babhala inkcazo, imbali yamaxesha ayamkelwa yi-caricatures. Iikopi ezininzi zoHlelo lweBohn ziye zahlulwa zahlulwa zaza zagqithiswa njengezoqobo (bona ukuQokelelwa ngezantsi). Nangona imiqulu emibini yoHlelo lweBohn ihlala iboniswa njengengqokelela epheleleyo yemisebenzi kaGillray, oku akunjalo: umzekelo, i-Doublûres of Characters ayiqukwanga kuyo nayiphi na ivolumu. Oku kunokwenzeka kakhulu ngenxa yokuba olu shicilelo aluzange lupapashwe nguHannah Humphrey, kodwa nguJohn Wright malunga noPhononongo lwe-Anti-Jacobin kunye neMagazini. 

Uhlelo olulandelayo, olunesihloko esithi Imisebenzi kaJames Gillray, iCaricaturist: kunye neBali loBomi bakhe kunye namaxesha (Chatto & Windus, 1874), yayingumsebenzi kaThomas Wright, [11] kwaye wazisa uGillray kuluntu olukhulu. Olu hlelo, olupheleleyo kumqulu omnye, luqulethe imifanekiso emibini kaGillray, nemizobo engaphezu kwama-400.[4]

Impembelelo 
uGillray isahlonitshwa njengenye yee-caricaturists zezopolitiko ezinempembelelo kulo lonke ixesha, kwaye phakathi kweekhathuni eziphambili kwinqanaba lezopolitiko e-United Kingdom namhlanje, bobabini uSteve Bell noMartin Rowson bayamvuma ukuba mhlawumbi wayenempembelelo enkulu kunabo bonke abanduleli babo kuloo ndawo [icatshulwa]. Unjingalwazi uDavid Taylor, ingcaphephe yeYunivesithi yaseToronto kwintlondi yezopolitiko, wathi ngo-2013, "Ngaphandle kombuzo, ukuba umzobi ohamba phambili ngelo xesha-uJames Gillray-wayebonise uRob Ford ngewayengenanceba kakhulu kunanamhlanje. 

" Umzobi wopopayi waseNew Zealand wenkulungwane yama-20 uDavid Low wachaza uHogarth njengoyisemkhulu yaye uGillray uyise womzobi wezopolitiko.[3] Ubuso beNkundla kaFlunkey kwiminyaka yoo-1980/1990 kamabonakude waseBritane ohlekisayo kanopopi umboniso weSpitting Image yicaricature kaGillray, ejongwe njengembeko kuyise wezopopayi zezopolitiko. [13] 

Kwinqaku elinomxholo othi Ukufundwa kwe-Rousseauian kwe-Gillray's National Conveniences uJohn Moores wabhala, "Njengomboniso weSizwe kunye nomboniso we-Fashion Mamma, uGillray wayenomdla kwiingcamango zikaRousseau, umsebenzi wakhe waphenjelelwa ngabo, kwaye, njengoko uyilo lwamva kwi-revolution kunye ne-radicalism lubonisa, wabamba uRousseau ngokubhekiselele ekuphakameni okuphezulu, esebenzisa enye impembelelo ye-revolution. kwimizobo yakhe yemibhalo kaRousseau.




Umzobi wekhathuni ngumzobi obonwayo osebenza ngokukhethekileyo ekuzobeni nasekubhaleni [1] imifanekiso eqingqiweyo (imifanekiso yomntu ngamnye) okanye iikhomikhi (imifanekiso elandelelanayo). Abazobi bekhathuni bohlukile kubabhali bamabali ahlekisayo okanye abenzi bemifanekiso/amagcisa ahlekisayo kuba bavelisa zombini iinxalenye zoncwadi kunye nemizobo yomsebenzi njengenxalenye yomsebenzi wabo. 

Abazobi basenokusebenza ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo, kuquka iincwadana, imifanekiso ehlekisayo, iincwadi ezihlekisayo, iikhathuni zomhleli, iinoveli zegraphic, iimanuwali, iikhathuni zegag, iibhodi zamabali, iipowusta, iihempe, iincwadi, izibhengezo, amakhadi okubulisa, iimagazini, amaphephandaba, iiwebcomics, kunye nokupakishwa komdlalo wevidiyo. 

Isigama 
Jonga kwakhona: Umyili weeKhomikhi 
Uqeqesho lomzobi wekhathuni lubandakanya iindlela zokugunyazisa kunye noyilo loyilo[1] (jonga ubugcisa obuhlukeneyo). Amagama athi "umzobi wemifanekiso ehlekisayo", "igcisa lemifanekiso ehlekisayo", okanye "igcisa lencwadi ehlekisayo" abhekisa kwinxalenye yokwenza imifanekiso yoqeqesho lwekhathuni[2] (jonga umzobi). Ngelixa wonke "umzobi wekhathuni" unokugqalwa "njengomzobi wemifanekiso ehlekisayo", "umzobi weencwadi ezihlekisayo", okanye "umzobi weencwadi ezihlekisayo", ingenguye wonke "umzobi weekhathuni", "igcisa leekhathuni", okanye "igcisa lencwadi ehlekisayo" ngumzobi "ngumzobi". 

Ukungacaci kakuhle kunokuvela xa abazobi nababhali besabelana ngemisebenzi yabo ekubhaleni umsebenzi.[3] 

Iikhathuni zembali 
yoHlelo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ikhathuni yoHlelo 
Umbhali weNgesi kunye nomzobi wekhathuni ongumhleli uWilliam Hogarth, owavela ngenkulungwane ye-18, wahlekisa ngezopolitiko namasiko alo xesha; imizekeliso yohlobo olunjalo idla ngokubizwa ngokuba yi "Hogarthian".[4] Ukulandela umsebenzi kaHogarth, iikhathuni zomhleli/kwezopolitiko zaqala ukukhula eNgilani ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-18 phantsi kolawulo lwabachasi bayo abakhulu, uJames Gillray noThomas Rowlandson, bobabini baseLondon. UGillray uphonononge ukusetyenziswa kwe-medium for lampooning kunye ne-caricature, ebiza ukumkani (uGeorge III), iinkulumbuso kunye neenjengele ukuba ziphendule, kwaye uye wabizwa ngokuba nguyise wekhathuni yezopolitiko.[5] 


UBenjamin Franklin's Joyina, okanye Die (ngoMeyi 9, 1754), ugqalwa njengekhathuni yokuqala epapashwe kwiphephandaba laseMelika 
Imvelaphi e-US 
Ngelixa engazange abe ngumzobi ochwepheshile, uBenjamin Franklin unikwa imbeko ngekhathuni yokuqala eyapapashwa kwiGazethi yasePennsylvania ngoMeyi 9, 1754: Joyina, okanye Die, ebonisa iikoloni zaseMelika njengeenxalenye [6]. Ngenkulungwane ye-19, abadwebi oopopayi abaziingcali ezifana noThomas Nast, omsebenzi wakhe wavela kwi-Harper's Weekly, wazisa ezinye iisimboli eziqhelekileyo zezopolitiko zaseMelika, njengendlovu yeRiphabhlikhi. [6] 

Imicu yeKhomikhi 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-Comic strip I- 
Comic 



icons I-Comic portal 
vte 
Imicu ehlekisayo ifumene ukusasazwa ngokubanzi kumaphephandaba aqhelekileyo ngamaqumrhu.[8]

UCalum MacKenzie, kwintshayelelo yakhe kwikhathalogu yomboniso, I-Scottish Cartoonists (iGlasgow Print Studio Gallery, 1979) ichaze indlela yokukhetha: 

Umahluko phakathi komdwebi wekhathuni kunye nomzobi wemifanekiso wawufana nokwahluko phakathi komdlali ohlekisayo kunye nomdlali we-comedy-owayengaphambili bobabini bahambisa imigca yabo kwaye bathathe uxanduva olupheleleyo emva kokuba indalo yakhe yonke yayingenakuyifihla yonke into. 
Imicu emininzi ibingumsebenzi wabantu ababini nangona bekubonisiwe umsayino omnye kuphela. Kungekudala emva kokuba uFrank Willard eqale i-Moon Mullins ngo-1923, waqesha uFerd Johnson njengomncedisi wakhe. Kwiminyaka emininzi, uJohnson akazange afumane tyala. UWillard noJohnson bahamba malunga neFlorida, iMaine, iLos Angeles, kunye neMexico, bezoba umtya ngelixa behlala ezihotele, ezindlini nasezifama. Kwincopho yayo yokuduma ngeminyaka yoo-1940 kunye neyee-1950, lo mcu wakhutshwa kumaphephandaba angama-350. Ngokutsho kukaJohnson, wayesenza i-strip solo ubuncinane iminyaka elishumi ngaphambi kokufa kukaWillard kwi-1958: "Babeka igama lam ngoko. Ndandiyenza malunga neminyaka eyi-10 ngaphambi koko kuba uWillard wayenokuhlaselwa yintliziyo kunye nokubetha kunye nazo zonke ezo zinto. Ngomzuzu igama lam lahamba kuloo nto kwaye igama lakhe lahamba, amaphepha e-25 awela umgca. Oko kubonisa ukuba igama le-10 lithetha ukuba, nangona kunjalo, igama le-10 lithetha oko, nangona kunjalo 









. ubugcisa ziindlela zobugcisa ezifana nokupeyinta, ukuzoba, ukwenziwa koshicilelo, ukukrola, iiseramikhi, ukufota, ividiyo, imifanekiso, ukwenza iifilim, uyilo, ubugcisa kunye noyilo lwezakhiwo. Amacandelo amaninzi obugcisa afana nobugcisa bokudlala, ubugcisa bokucinga, kunye nobugcisa bempahla elukiweyo, ikwabandakanya imiba yobugcisa obubonakalayo, kunye nobugcisa bezinye iindidi. Ngaphakathi kobugcisa obubonakalayo, [1] ubugcisa obusetyenzisiweyo, [2] obufana noyilo lwemizi-mveliso, uyilo lomzobo, uyilo lwefashoni, uyilo lwangaphakathi, kunye nobugcisa bokuhombisa[3] nazo zibandakanyiwe. 

Usetyenziso lwangoku lwegama elithi "ubugcisa obubonwayo" bubandakanya ubugcisa obuhle kunye nokusetyenziswa okanye ubugcisa bokuhombisa kunye nobugcisa, kodwa oku bekungasoloko kunjalo. Phambi kweNtshukumo yobuGcisa nobuGcisa eBritani nakwezinye iindawo ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, igama elithi 'igcisa' kangangeenkulungwane ezithile lalisoloko lithintelwa kuphela umntu osebenza kubugcisa obuhle (njengokupeyinta, ukukrola, okanye ukwenza ushicilelo) hayi ubugcisa bokuhombisa, ubugcisa, okanye ukusebenzisa amajelo osasazo obugcisa. Lo mahluko wagxininiswa ngamagcisa eNtshukumo yobuGcisa neMisebenzi yeMisebenzi, exabise iindlela zobugcisa zeelwimi zasekuhlaleni kangangoko ziphezulu.[4] Izikolo zobugcisa zawenza mahluko phakathi kwezobugcisa nezezandla, zigcina ukuba umntu oqeqeshelwe ukwenza umsebenzi wezandla akanakugqalwa njengengcali yobugcisa.

Ukuthambekela okwandayo kwilungelo lokupeyinta, kwaye ukuya kwinqanaba elingaphantsi kwemifanekiso eqingqiweyo, ngaphezu kobunye ubugcisa ibe yinkalo yobugcisa baseNtshona kunye nobugcisa base-East Asia. Kuyo yomibini le mimandla, ukupeyinta kubonwe njengokuthembela kwelona qondo liphezulu kwintelekelelo yegcisa nokuba lelona lide lisuswe emsebenzini wezandla – kwimizobo yaseTshayina, ezona ndlela zixatyiswe kakhulu yayizezo "zokupenda kwabafundi", ubuncinci ngokwethiyori eyenziwa ngabafundi abangabaziyo. Uluhlu lwaseNtshona lweentlobo lubonise izimo zengqondo ezifanayo. 

Imfundo noqeqesho 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imfundo yobugcisa obubonakalayo 
Uqeqesho kubugcisa obubonwayo ngokubanzi belusenziwa ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo zabafundi abafunda umsebenzi kunye neenkqubo zocweyo. EYurophu, intshukumo yeRenaissance yokwandisa iwonga legcisa ikhokelele kwinkqubo yeakhademi yokuqeqesha amagcisa, kwaye namhlanje uninzi lwabantu abalandela ikhondo loqeqesho lobugcisa kwizikolo zobugcisa kumanqanaba emfundo ephakamileyo. Ubugcisa obubonwayo ngoku buye baba sisifundo esikhethwayo kwiinkqubo ezininzi zemfundo.[5][6] 

KwiMpuma yeAsia, imfundo yobugcisa yamagcisa angengowomsebenzi idla ngokujolisa kwibrashi; i-calligraphy yayibalwa phakathi koBugcisa obuSithandathu bamanene kwi-Chinese Zhou dynasty, kunye ne-calligraphy kunye nokupeyinta kwamaTshayina babalelwa phakathi kwezobugcisa ezine zamagosa e-China yobukhosi.[7][8][9] 

Ilizwe elihamba phambili ekuphuhliseni ubugcisa eLatin America, kwi-1875 yakha i-National Society of the Stimulus of the Arts, eyasungulwa ngabadwebi u-Eduardo Schiaffino, u-Eduardo Sívori, kunye nabanye abaculi. Umbutho wabo waphinda waqanjwa njenge-National Academy of Fine Arts kwi-1905 kwaye, kwi-1923, kwinqanaba lomzobi kunye nomfundi u-Ernesto de la Cárcova, njengesebe kwiYunivesithi yaseBuenos Aires, i-Superior Art School yeSizwe. Okwangoku, umbutho okhokelayo wezemfundo wezobugcisa kweli lizwe yi-UNA Universidad Nacional de las Artes.[10] 

Umzobo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umzobo 
Umzobo oneenkcukacha zomzobo wasetyhini onesihloko esithi 'Extinction' nguChristiaan Tonnis, owadalwa ngo-1981 enegraphite neepensile ezinemibala, enobukhulu obuyi-13.6 x 18.5 intshi. Ika-Kunstverein Familie Montez ukusukela ngoDisemba 2010. 
UChristiaan Tonnis - IQhawe loMfazi #14 'Extinction', ipensile kunye nepensile enemibala ephepheni, 1981
Umzobo yindlela yokwenza umfanekiso, umzobo okanye umzobo usebenzisa naziphi na iintlobo ngeentlobo zezixhobo kunye nobuchule obukhoyo kwi-intanethi nangaphandle kweintanethi. Ibandakanya ngokubanzi ukwenza amanqaku kumphezulu ngokusebenzisa uxinzelelo olusuka kwisixhobo, okanye ukususa isixhobo kumhlaba wonke kusetyenziswa imidiya eyomileyo efana neepensile zegraphite, ipeni kunye ne-inki, iibhrashi zeinki, iipensile zombala wewax, iikhrayoni, amalahle, iipastel, kunye neziphawuli. Izixhobo zedijithali, kubandakanywa iipeni, i-stylus, ezilinganisa iziphumo zezi nazo zisetyenziswa. Amacebo aphambili asetyenziswayo ekuzobeni zezi: ukuzoba umgca, ukuqandusela, ukuqandusela, ukuqandusela ngokungacwangciswanga, ukukhuhla, ukukrwela, ukuqhotsa, kunye nokudibanisa. Umzobi ogqwesileyo ekuzobeni ubizwa ngokuba ngumzobi okanye umzobi.[11] 
i-Nefertari kunye ne-Isis

Ukuzoba nokupeyinta kubuyela emva kumashumi amawaka eminyaka.[12] Ubugcisa be-Upper Paleolithic bubandakanya ubugcisa bomfuziselo obuqala ubuncinci kwiminyaka eyi-40,000 eyadlulayo.[13] Imizobo yomqolomba engeyiyo eyomfuziselo equka izigxina zezandla kunye neemilo zejometri ezilula zindala nangakumbi.[12] Ukumelwa emqolombeni Paleolithic zezilwanyana zifumaneka kwiindawo ezifana Lascaux, France, Altamira, Spain, [14] Maros, Sulawesi e Asia, [15] kunye Gabarnmung, Australia [16]. 

KwiYiputa yamandulo, imizobo ye-inki kumpapiri, ngokufuthi ebonisa abantu, yayisetyenziswa njengemizekelo yokuzoba okanye yokukrola.[17] Imizobo kwiivazi zesiGrike, ekuqaleni zejometri, kamva zaphuhliswa zibe yimo yomntu ngobudongwe obunomfanekiso omnyama ngenkulungwane yesi-6 BC.[18] 

Ngephepha eliye laxhaphaka ngakumbi eYurophu ngenkulungwane ye-14, [19] umzobo wamkelwa ziinkosi ezinjengoSandro Botticelli, uRaphael, uMichelangelo, noLeonardo da Vinci, owathi maxa wambi wayephatha umzobo njengobugcisa ngokwawo, kunokuba ube linqanaba lokulungiselela ukupeyinta okanye umzobo.[20] 

Ukupeyinta 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukupeyinta 
Ipeyinti ethathwa ngokoqobo luqheliselo lokusebenzisa i-pigment exhonywe kwi-carrier (okanye medium) kunye ne-agent ebophelelayo (iglu) kumphezulu (inkxaso) efana nephepha, i-canvas okanye udonga. Nangona kunjalo, xa isetyenziswe kwingqiqo yobugcisa ithetha ukusetyenziswa kwalo msebenzi ngokudibanisa nomzobo, ukwakheka, okanye ezinye iingqalelo zobuhle ukuze kubonakaliswe injongo ecacileyo kunye nengqiqo yengcali. Ukupeyinta kukwasetyenziselwa ukuvakalisa imimoya kunye neengcamango zomoya; iisayithi zolu hlobo lokupeyinta ukusuka kwimizobo ebonisa imifanekiso yasentsomini kwizinto zomdongwe ukuya kwiSistine Chapel, ukuya kumzimba womntu ngokwawo.[21] 

Imbali 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yokupeyinta 
Imvelaphi kunye nembali yokuqala 

umzobo weLascaux 

Njengomzobo, ukupeyinta kunemvelaphi ebhaliweyo kwimiqolomba nakubuso bamatye. [22] Imizobo yokuqala eyaziwayo emqolombeni, eyaqala phakathi kweminyaka engama-32,000-30,000 eyadlulayo, ifumaneka kumqolomba we-Chauvet kumazantsi eFransi;[23] imizobo eseludongeni edumileyo yaseLascaux ifikelele kwiminyaka eyi-17,000–15,500 eyadlulayo.[24] Kwimithunzi ebomvu, emdaka, emthubi namnyama, imizobo eseludongeni kunye neesilingi ibonisa iinyathi, iinkomo (ii-aurochs), amahashe namaxhama.[25] 

Imizobo yemifanekiso yabantu inokufumaneka kumangcwaba aseYiputa yamandulo. Kwitempile enkulu kaRamesses II, uNefertari, ukumkanikazi wakhe, uboniswa ekhokelwa nguIsis.[26] AmaGrike aba negalelo ekupeyinteni kodwa uninzi lomsebenzi wabo ulahlekile. Olunye lolona phawu lubalaseleyo lushiyekileyo yimizobo yomama ye-Hellenistic Fayum. Omnye umzekelo ngumfanekiso oqingqiweyo weDabi laseIssus ePompeii, ekusenokwenzeka ukuba lalisekelwe kumzobo wamaGrike. Ubugcisa bamaGrike namaRoma baba negalelo kubugcisa baseByzantium ngenkulungwane yesi-4 ngaphambi kweXesha lethu Eliqhelekileyo, nto leyo eyaqalisa isithethe kwimizobo yemifanekiso. [27] Inqaku eliphambili 

leRenaissance 
: umzobo weRenaissance yaseItali
Ngaphandle kwemibhalo-ngqangi ekhanyisiweyo eyaveliswa ziimonki ebudeni bamaXesha Aphakathi, igalelo elibalulekileyo elilandelayo kubugcisa baseYurophu yaba ngabapeyinti bokuvuselelwa ngokutsha kweItali. Ukusuka eGiotto ngenkulungwane ye-13 ukuya kuLeonardo da Vinci kunye noRaphael ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-16, eli yayilelona xesha lityebileyo kubugcisa baseTaliyane njengoko ubuchule be-chiaroscuro basetyenziswa ukwenza inkohliso yendawo ye-3-D.[28] 

Abazobi bakumntla Yurophu nabo baphenjelelwa sisikolo saseItali. UJan van Eyck waseBelgium, uPieter Bruegel oMdala waseNetherlands kunye noHans Holbein oMnci waseJamani baphakathi kwabapeyinti abanempumelelo kula maxesha. Basebenzise ubuchule bokukhenkceza ngeeoyile ukufikelela ubunzulu kunye nokukhanya. 

Iinkosi zaseDatshi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umzobo weDutch Golden Age 
kaRembrandt wokupeyinta Ubusuku Bukela amadoda amabini egxalathelana phambili nesihlwele 
Rembrandt: I-Night Watch, 1642 
Inkulungwane ye-17 yabona ukuvela kweengcungela ezinkulu zamaDatshi ezifana noRembrandt oguquguqukayo owayekhunjulwa ngokukodwa ngemifanekiso yakhe kunye nemiboniso yeBhayibhile, kunye noVermeer okhethekileyo kwimiboniso yobomi baseDatshi. Inqaku 

leBaroque 
eliPhambili: IBaroque 
IBaroque yaqala emva kweRenaissance, ukusuka ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-16 ukuya ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-17. Amagcisa aphambili eBaroque aquka uCaravaggio, owasebenzisa kakhulu i-tenebrism. UPeter Paul Rubens, umzobi waseFlemish owafunda eItali, wasebenzela iicawa zasekuhlaleni e-Antwerp kwaye wapeyinta uthotho lukaMarie de' Medici. U-Annibale Carracci wathatha iimpembelelo kwiSistine Chapel kwaye wenza uhlobo lwepeyinti yesilingi ekhohlisayo. Uninzi lwenkqubela phambili eyenzeka kwiBaroque yayingenxa yoHlaziyo lwamaProtestanti kunye nesiphumo sokuLwa koHlaziyo. Uninzi lwento echaza iBaroque kukukhanya okumangalisayo kunye nokubonwayo ngokubanzi.[29] 

Impressionism 
Inqaku eliphambili: Impressionism 
Inqaku eliphambili le 
-Post-impressionism : I-Post-Impressionism

Claude Monet: Impression, Sunrise (1872) 
Impressionism yaqala eFransi ngenkulungwane ye-19 kunye nombutho okhululekileyo wamagcisa aquka uClaude Monet, uPierre-Auguste Renoir kunye noPaul Cézanne abazise isimbo esitsha ngokukhululekileyo sokupeyinta, ngokufuthi bekhetha ukupeyinta imiboniso eyinyani yobomi banamhlanje ngaphandle kune studio. Oku kwaphunyezwa ngokubonakaliswa okutsha kweempawu zobuhle ezibonakaliswe ngokubethwa kwebrashi kunye nokubonakala kokwenyani. Baye bazuza ukungcangcazela kombala okunzulu ngokusebenzisa imibala esulungekileyo, engaxutywanga kunye nemivumbo emfutshane yebrashi. Intshukumo yaphembelela ubugcisa njengento eguquguqukayo, ehamba ngexesha kunye nohlengahlengiso kubuchule obutsha kunye nombono wobugcisa. Ukuthathela ingqalelo kwiinkcukacha kuye kwaba yinto ephambili ekuphunyezweni, ngelixa kuphononongwa umbono ocalanye wembonakalo yomhlaba kunye nendalo kwiliso legcisa. [30][31] 

Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, abapeyinti abaliqela abancinci bathatha i-impressionism ukuya kwinqanaba elingaphezulu, besebenzisa iimo zejometri kunye nombala ongaqhelekanga ukubonisa iimvakalelo ngelixa bezama ukufumana isimboli esinzulu. Okuphawuleka ngokukhethekileyo nguPaul Gauguin, owaphenjelelwa kakhulu yi-Asia, Afrika kunye nobugcisa baseJapan, uVincent van Gogh, umDatshi owafudukela eFransi apho wazoba khona ukukhanya kwelanga okunamandla emazantsi, kunye neToulouse-Lautrec, ekhunjulwayo ngenxa yemizobo yakhe ecacileyo yobomi basebusuku kwisithili saseParis saseMontmartre. [32] 

ISimbolism, i-expressionism kunye ne-cubism 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ubugcisa bale mihla 
uEdvard Munch, igcisa laseNorway, waphuhlisa indlela yakhe yomfuziselo ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19, ephefumlelwe nguManet obonisa umbono waseFransi. I-Scream (1893), owona msebenzi wakhe udumileyo, utolikwa ngokubanzi njengomele ixhala lehlabathi lomntu wale mihla. Ngokuyinxenye ngenxa yempembelelo kaMunch, intshukumo yaseJamani yokubonakalisa intetho yavela eJamani ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 njengoko amagcisa anjengoErnst Kirschner kunye no-Erich Heckel baqala ukugqwetha inyaniso ngempembelelo yeemvakalelo. 

Ngokunxuseneyo, isitayile esaziwa ngokuba yi-cubism esaphuhliswa eFransi njengamagcisa agxile kumthamo kunye nendawo yezakhiwo ezibukhali ngaphakathi kokwakheka. UPablo Picasso kunye noGeorges Braque babengabasekeli abahamba phambili bentshukumo. Izinto ziyaqhawuka, zihlalutywe, kwaye ziphinde zidityaniswe ngendlela ecatshulweyo. Ngeminyaka yee-1920, isimbo sasisele siphuhliswe saba yi-surrealism kunye noDali noMagritte. [33] 

Ukwenziwa koShicilelo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukwenziwa koShicilelo 
Umkrolo wamaTshayina wamandulo wababetheli bezixhobo ababhinqileyo 
Umkrolo wamandulo wamaTshayina wabadlali bezixhobo ababhinqileyo 
Ukwenza ushicilelo kuyila, ngeenjongo zobugcisa, umfanekiso okwimatrix othi ukhutshelwe kumphezulu omacala mabini (flat) nge-inki okanye olunye uhlobo lombala.[34] Ngaphandle kwimeko ye-monotype, i-matrix efanayo ingasetyenziselwa ukuvelisa imizekelo emininzi yoshicilelo.[35]

Ngokwembali, obona buchule buphambili (abakwabizwa ngokuba yimithombo yeendaba) kukwenza umthi, [36] ukukrola umgca, [37] ukukrolwa, [38] lithography, [39] kunye noshicilelo lwesikrini, [40] (serigraphy, isilika screening) kwaye kukho ezinye ezininzi, kubandakanywa ubuchule bedijithali.[41] Ngokwesiqhelo, ushicilelo lushicilelwa ephepheni,[19] kodwa ezinye iindlela zokusebenzelana zisukela kwilaphu kunye nevellum,[42] ukuya kwimathiriyeli yangoku ngakumbi.[43] 
 
Imbali yaseYurophu 
Inqaku eliphambili: Iprinta yenkosi endala
Ushicilelo kwisithethe saseNtshona olwaveliswa ngaphambi kowe-1830 zaziwa njengeempapasho zakudala eziphambili. EYurophu, ukusuka malunga ne-1400 AD umthi womthi, wawusetyenziselwa ukuprinta okukhulu ephepheni kusetyenziswa ubuchule bokushicilela obuphuhliswe kwilizwe laseByzantium kunye ne-Islamic. UMichael Wolgemut waphucula ukucandwa kwemithi yaseJamani ukususela malunga nowe-1475, yaye uErhard Reuwich, umDatshi, waba ngowokuqala ukusebenzisa ukuqandusela. Ekupheleni kwenkulungwane u-Albrecht Dürer wazisa i-Western woodcut kwinqanaba elingazange ligqithwe, linyusa iwonga le-woodcut yegqabi elinye.[44] 

Imvelaphi nokusebenza kwamaTshayina 
I-Chinese Diamond Sutra, eyona ncwadi indala yehlabathi yoshicilelo ye-Woodblock ukususela ngowama-868 CE 
I-Chinese Diamond Sutra, eyona ncwadi indala ehlabathini eshicilelweyo (868 CE) 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukuprintwa kwe-Woodblock 
E-China, ubugcisa bokwenza ushicilelo baphuhliswa kwiminyaka eli-1,100 eyadlulayo njengemizobo ehambisana nesicatshulwa esisikwe kwiiplanga ukuze siprintwe ephepheni. Ekuqaleni imifanekiso yayiyeyonqulo ubukhulu becala kodwa kumnombo weNgoma, amagcisa aqalisa ukusika imbonakalo yomhlaba. Ngexesha le-Ming (1368-1644) kunye ne-Qing (1616-1911) dynasties, ubuchule bobuchwephesha bugqibelele kwimizobo yenkolo kunye neyobugcisa.[45][46] 

Uphuhliso eJapan, ngo-1603–1867 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ushicilelo lweWoodblock eJapan 
Hokusai umbala woshicilelo "I-Fuji ebomvu yomoya wasemzantsi ocacileyo kusasa" ukusuka kwiMibono engamashumi amathathu anesithandathu yeMount Fuji 
Hokusai: I-Fuji eBomvu ukusuka kwiMibono engamashumi amathathu anesithandathu yeNtaba iFuji (1830-1832) 
iWoodblock yoshicilelo eJapani, iHakunga yaseJapan ubuchule obaziwa kakhulu ngokusetyenziswa kwabo kudidi lobugcisa be ukiyo-e; noko ke, yayisetyenziswa ngokubanzi kakhulu ekushicileleni iincwadi ezinemifanekiso kwangelo xesha linye. Ushicilelo lweWoodblock lwalusetyenziswa eTshayina kangangeenkulungwane ukushicilela iincwadi, kwakudala ngaphambi kokuvela kohlobo olushukumayo, kodwa lwamkelwa ngokubanzi eJapan ngexesha le-Edo (1603–1867).[47][48] Nangona ifana neplanga kwi-western printmaking kwezinye izinto, i-moku hanga ihluke kakhulu kwii-inki ezisekelwe emanzini zisetyenziswa (ngokuchasene ne-Western woodcut, esebenzisa i-oyile esekelwe kwi-oyile), evumela uluhlu olubanzi lombala ocacileyo, ukukhenkceza kunye nokubonakala kombala.

Emva kokuhla kwe-ukiyo-e kunye nokuqaliswa kobuchwepheshe bokushicilela banamhlanje, ukushicilelwa kwe-woodblock kwaqhubeka njengendlela yokushicilela izicatshulwa kunye nokuvelisa ubugcisa, zombini kwiindlela zendabuko ezifana ne-ukiyo-e kunye neentlobo ezahlukeneyo ze-radical okanye zaseNtshona ezinokuthi zithathwe njengobugcisa bale mihla. Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, i-shin-hanga eyadibanisa isithethe sika ukiyo-e kunye nobuchule bemizobo yaseNtshona yaduma, kwaye imisebenzi kaHasui Kawase noHiroshi Yoshida yafumana ukuthandwa kumazwe ngamazwe. [49] [50] Amaziko afana ne "Adachi Institute of Woodblock Prints" kunye ne "Takezasado" ayaqhubeka nokuvelisa ushicilelo lwe-ukiyo-e kunye nezinto ezifanayo kunye neendlela ezazisetyenziswa kwixesha elidlulileyo. [51] [52] 
 
Ukufota 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukufota
Ukufota yinkqubo yokwenza imifanekiso ngokwenza ukukhanya. Iipateni zokukhanya ezibonakalisiweyo okanye ezikhutshwa kwizinto zirekhodwa kwindawo enovakalelo, okanye itshiphu yokugcina, ngokutyhileka kwexesha.[53] Inkqubo yenziwa ngezivalo ezingoomatshini [54] okanye ukuvezwa kwe-electronic kwangexesha kweefotoni zibe yinkqubo yekhemikhali okanye izixhobo ezifakwa kwidijithali ezaziwa ngokuba ziikhamera.[55] 

Eli gama lisuka kwisiGrike φῶς ''phos'' (“ukukhanya”) kunye γραφή ''graphê'' (“umzobo” okanye “ukubhala”), ngokoqobo elithetha “ukuzoba ngokukhanya”.[56] Ngokwesithethe, imveliso yokufota ibizwa ngokuba yifoto; Igama elithi ''ifoto'' sisishunqulelo kwaye nangona abaninzi beyibiza ngokuba "yimifanekiso," igama elithi "umfanekiso" liye lathatha indawo "ifoto," ebonisa ukuthathwa kwe-elektroniki kunye nengqikelelo ebanzi yokumelwa komzobo kwi-optics nakwicomputing.[57] 

Uyilo lwezakhiwo 
Bona kwakhona: Uluhlu lwesoftware yeBIM 

yezindlu ezenziwe ngamaplanga eBrittany 
Architecture yinkqubo kunye nemveliso yokucwangcisa, ukuyila, kunye nokwakha izakhiwo okanye naziphi na ezinye izakhiwo.[58] Imisebenzi yoyilo, ngohlobo lwezakhiwo, idla ngokubonwa njengemiqondiso yenkcubeko kunye nemisebenzi yobugcisa.[59] Iimbali zempucuko zihlala zichongwa kunye nempumelelo yazo eseleyo yezakhiwo.[60] 

Umsebenzi obhaliweyo wokuqala owasindayo kwi-architecture yi-De Architectura, ngumakhi waseRoma uVitruvius ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yoku-1 AD.[61] Ngokutsho kukaVitruvius, isakhiwo esilungileyo sifanele sanelise imigaqo emithathu: firmitas, utilitas, venustas, iguqulelwe njengokuqina, imveliso, nolonwabo.[62] Into elinganayo kwisiNgesi sanamhlanje iya kuba: 

Ukuqina - isakhiwo kufuneka sime ngamandla kwaye sihlale sikwimeko entle. 
I-Utility - kufuneka ilungele iinjongo esetyenziselwa yona. 
Ubuhle - kufuneka bube nomtsalane ngokwembonakalo. [63] 
Ukwakha kuqala kwavela kutshintsho phakathi kweemfuno (ikhusi, ukhuseleko, unqulo, njl.njl.) kunye neendlela (izinto zokwakha ezikhoyo kunye nezakhono zomlindi).[64] Njengoko iinkcubeko ziphuhliswa kunye nolwazi lwaqala ukumiselwa ngokusesikweni ngezithethe zomlomo kunye nezenzo, ukwakha kwaba yinto yobugcisa, kwaye "ubugcisa bokwakha" ligama elinikwe kwezona nguqulelo zisesikweni kakhulu zezo zandla.[65] 

Ukwenziwa kwefilimu 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukwenza ifilimu 
Ukwenza ifilimu yinkqubo yokwenza umfanekiso oshukumayo, ukususela ekukhawulweni kokuqala kunye nophando, ngokubhala isikripthi, ukudubula kunye nokurekhoda, i-animation okanye ezinye iziphumo ezikhethekileyo, ukuhlela, isandi kunye nomsebenzi womculo kwaye ekugqibeleni usasazwe kubaphulaphuli; ibhekisa ngokubanzi ekudalweni kwazo zonke iintlobo zeefilim, ukwamkela i-documentary, iintlobo zethiyetha kunye noncwadi kwifilimu, kunye nemibongo okanye yovavanyo, kwaye ihlala isetyenziselwa ukubhekisa kwiinkqubo ezisekelwe kwividiyo ngokunjalo. 

Umzobo weKhompyutha 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ubugcisa beKhompyutha 
Jonga kwakhona: Ubugcisa beDijithali 

uDesmond Paul Henry, uMfanekiso ngoMatshini wokuzoba 1, c. 1960
Amagcisa abonwayo awasekho kuphela kumajelo eendaba obugcisa obubonwayo bemveli. Iikhompyutha ziye zasetyenziswa kubugcisa obubonakalayo ukususela ngeminyaka yoo-1960. [66] Usebenziso lubandakanya ukubamba okanye ukuyilwa kwemifanekiso kunye neefom, [67] ukuhlelwa kwaloo mifanekiso (kubandakanywa nokuphonononga iingoma ezininzi) [68] kunye nonikezelo lokugqibela okanye ushicilelo (kuquka ushicilelo lwe-3D).[69] 

Ubugcisa bekhompyutha yiyo nayiphi na indima apho iikhompyutha zidlala indima kwimveliso okanye ekuboniseni.[70] Ubugcisa obunjalo bunokuba ngumfanekiso, isandi, oopopayi, ividiyo, iCD-ROM, iDVD, umdlalo wevidiyo, iwebhusayithi, i-algorithm, ukusebenza okanye ukufakwa kwegalari.[71] 

Izifundo ezininzi zemveli ngoku zidibanisa ubugcisa bedijithali, ngoko ke imigca phakathi kwemisebenzi yemveli yobugcisa kunye nemisebenzi yemidiya emitsha eyenziwe kusetyenziswa iikhompyutha iye yaluzizi.[72] Umzekelo, umzobi unokudibanisa umzobo wemveli kunye nobugcisa be-algorithmic kunye nobunye ubuchule bedijithali. [73] Ngenxa yoko, ukuchaza ubugcisa bekhompyuter ngemveliso yayo yokugqibela kunokuba nzima. Nangona kunjalo, olu hlobo lobugcisa luvela kwimiboniso yemyuziyam yobugcisa, kodwa inokubonwa ngakumbi njengesixhobo, kunokuba ifom efana nokupeyinta.[74] Kwelinye icala, kukho imizobo esekwe kwikhompyuter eyeyengcamango entsha kunye ne-postdigital strand, ethatha itekhnoloji efanayo, kunye nefuthe labo lentlalo, njengento yophando. [75] 

Ukusetyenziswa kweKhompyutha kuwenze mfiliba umahluko phakathi kwabazobi, abafoti, abahleli beefoto, abamodeli be-3-D, kunye namagcisa emisebenzi yezandla.[76] Unikezelo oluphucukileyo kunye nesoftware yokuhlela ikhokelele kubaphuhlisi bemifanekiso abanezakhono ezininzi. Abafoti banokuba ngamagcisa edijithali. [77] Imifanekiso eqingqiweyo isenokuba oopopayi. Ubugcisa bezandla busenokuncediswa ngekhompyutha okanye busebenzise imifanekiso eyenziwe ngekhompyutha njengomzekelo.[78] Ukusetyenziswa kobugcisa bekliphu yekhompyuter yenze umahluko phakathi kobugcisa obubonakalayo kunye noyilo lwephepha lucace gca ngenxa yofikelelo olulula kunye nokuhlelwa kobugcisa bekliphu kwinkqubo yokwenza iphepha kuxwebhu.[79] 

Ubugcisa bePlastiki 
Sculpture 
Inqaku eliphambili: Sculpture. 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ubugcisa bePlastiki
Ubugcisa bePlastiki ligama leefom zobugcisa ezibandakanya ukuphathwa ngokwasemzimbeni kwesixhobo seplastiki ngokubumba okanye ukwenza imodeli efana nomkroli okanye iiseramikhi. Eli gama likwasetyenziswa kuzo zonke izinto ezibonwayo (ezingezoncwadi, ezingezomculo) ubugcisa.[80][81] 

Izinto ezinokuthi ziqingqwe okanye zenziwe, njengelitye, umthi, ikhonkrithi, okanye intsimbi, nazo zibandakanyiwe kwinkcazo encinci, ekubeni, ngezixhobo ezifanelekileyo, ezo zinto ziyakwazi ukumodulation.[82] Oku kusetyenziswa kwegama elithi "iplastiki" kubugcisa kwahlukile kusetyenziso lukaPiet Mondrian, kunye nentshukumo awayibiza ngokuthi, "Neoplasticism."[83][84] 

Umfanekiso oqingqiweyo ngumsebenzi wobugcisa obuthathu owenziwe ngokubumba okanye ukudibanisa izinto ezinzima okanye zeplastiki, isandi, okanye isicatshulwa kunye okanye ukukhanya, ngokuqhelekileyo ilitye (ilitye okanye ilitye lebhastile), ilitye, iglasi, isinyithi, isinyithi, isinyithi. Eminye imifanekiso eqingqiweyo yenziwa ngokuthe ngqo ngokufumana okanye ngokukrola; ezinye zidityaniswe, zakhiwe kunye zize zitshiswe, zitshiswe, zibunjwe, okanye zenziwe. Imifanekiso eqingqiweyo idla ngokupeyintwa.[85] Umntu owenza imifanekiso eqingqiweyo kuthiwa ngumkroli. 

Imizekelo yokuqala engenakuphikiswa yemifanekiso eqingqiweyo yeyenkcubeko ye-Aurignacian, eyayiseYurophu nakumazantsi-ntshona e-Asia kwaye isebenza ekuqaleni kwe-Upper Paleolithic. Kunye nokuvelisa imizobo yokuqala eyaziwayo emqolombeni, abantu bale nkcubeko baphuhlise izixhobo zamatye eziyilwe ngokucokisekileyo, iipendenti zokwenziwa, izacholo, amaso eendlovu, nefluti yamathambo, kunye nemifanekiso enemigangatho emithathu.[86][87][88] 

Ngenxa yokuba umzobo ubandakanya ukusetyenziswa kwezixhobo ezinokubunjwa okanye ukumodareyithwa, kuthathwa njengenye yobugcisa beplastiki. Uninzi lobugcisa boluntu yimifanekiso eqingqiweyo. Imifanekiso eqingqiweyo emininzi kunye kwisitiya segadi inokubizwa ngokuba yigadi eqingqiweyo. Abakroli abasoloko besenza imizobo ngesandla. Ngokunyuka kwetekhnoloji kwinkulungwane yama-20 kunye nokuthandwa kobugcisa bengcinga ngaphezulu kobuchule bobugcisa, abakroli abaninzi bajikela kubenzi bobugcisa ukuze bavelise imisebenzi yabo yobugcisa. Ngokuqulunqwa, umzobi udala uyilo kwaye ahlawule umenzi wemveliso ukuba ayivelise. Oku kuvumela abakroli ukuba benze imifanekiso eqingqiweyo emikhulu kunye neyinkimbinkimbi ngakumbi kwizinto ezifana nesamente, isinyithi kunye neplastiki, abangenakukwazi ukuyidala ngesandla. Imifanekiso eqingqiweyo ingenziwa kwakhona ngeteknoloji yoshicilelo lwe-3-d. 

Inkcazo yelungelo lokushicilela lase-US lobugcisa obubonakalayo 
e-United States, umthetho okhusela ilungelo lokushicilela phezu kweqhekeza lobugcisa obubonakalayo unika inkcazo engqongqo ngakumbi "yobugcisa obubonakalayo".[89] 

"Umsebenzi wobugcisa obubonakalayo" ngu - 
(1) umzobo, umzobo, ushicilelo okanye umfanekiso oqingqiweyo, okhoyo kwikopi enye, kuhlelo olulinganiselweyo lweekopi ezingama-200 okanye ezimbalwa ezisayiniweyo kwaye zinomboliswe ngokulandelelana ngumbhali, okanye, kwimeko yomfanekiso oqingqiweyo, kwimifanekiso emininzi, eqingqiweyo, okanye eqingqwe kwimifanekiso eqingqiweyo ye-200 okanye i-signer kunye nenani le-200 olunye uphawu lombhali; okanye
(2) umfanekiso osafotayo oveliswe ngeenjongo zomboniso kuphela, okhoyo kwikopi enye esayinwe ngumbhali, okanye kuhlelo olulinganiselweyo lweekopi ezingama-200 okanye ezimbalwa ezisayiniweyo zaza zanombolwa ngokulandelelanayo ngumbhali. 

Umsebenzi wobugcisa obubonakalayo awubandakanyi — 
(A) (i) nayiphi na ipowusta, imephu, iglowubhu, itshati, umzobo wobugcisa, umzobo, imodeli, ubugcisa obusetyenzisiweyo, umfanekiso oshukumayo okanye omnye umsebenzi oviwayo, incwadi, iphephancwadi, iphephandaba, iperiodical, isiseko sedatha, inkonzo yolwazi lwe-elektroniki, upapasho lombane, okanye upapasho olufanayo; 
  (ii) nayiphi na into yokuthengisa okanye intengiso, intengiso, inkcazo, isigqubuthelo, okanye imathiriyeli yokupakisha okanye isingxobo; 
  (iii) nayiphi na inxalenye okanye inxalenye yayo nayiphi na into echazwe kwisolotya (i) okanye (ii); 
(B) nawuphi na umsebenzi owenzelwe ukuqeshwa; okanye 
(C) nawuphi na umsebenzi ongaxhomekekanga kukhuseleko lwelungelo lokushicilela phantsi kwesi sihloko.[89] 


Iicomics sisixhobo esisetyenziselwa ukuvakalisa izimvo ngemifanekiso, ehlala idityaniswa nesicatshulwa okanye olunye ulwazi olubonakalayo. Ithatha imo yolandelelwano lweephaneli zemifanekiso. Izixhobo zombhalo ezifana neebhaluni zentetho, ii-captions, ne- onomatopoeia zinokubonisa incoko, ukubalisa, isandi, okanye olunye ulwazi. Akukho mvumelwano phakathi kweethiyori kunye neembali-mlando malunga nenkcazo yee-comics; abanye bagxininisa ukudityaniswa kwemifanekiso kunye nokubhaliweyo, ulandelelwano oluthile okanye olunye unxulumano lomfanekiso, kunye neminye imiba yezembali efana nokuveliswa kobuninzi okanye ukusetyenziswa kwabalinganiswa abaphinda-phindayo. Ukuzoba iikhathuni kunye nezinye iindlela zokubonisa zezona ndlela ziqhelekileyo zokwenza imifanekiso kwiicomics. Iifoto ezihlekisayo luhlobo olusebenzisa imifanekiso yeefoto. Iifom eziqhelekileyo zibandakanya ii-comic strips, iikhathuni zokuhlela kunye ne-gag, kunye neencwadi ezihlekisayo. Ukusukela ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, imiqulu ebotshiweyo enjengeenoveli zegraphic, kunye neealbham ezihlekisayo, ziye zaxhaphaka, kunye neewebcomics.

Imbali yee-comics ilandele iindlela ezahlukeneyo kwiinkcubeko ezahlukeneyo. Abaphengululi baye babeka imbali yangaphambili ukuya kuthi ga kwimizobo yaseLascaux emqolombeni. Phakathi kwinkulungwane yama-20, amabali ahlekisayo aye ahambela phambili, ngokukodwa eUnited States, entshona Yurophu (ingakumbi iFransi neBelgium) naseJapan. Imbali yamabali ahlekisayo aseYurophu isoloko ilandwa kwiikhathuni zikaRodolphe Töpffer ngeminyaka yoo-1830s, ngelixa uWilhelm Busch kunye noMax wakhe noMoritz nabo babenempembelelo yehlabathi ukusukela ngo-1865 ukuya phambili, [1] [2] [3] [4] kwaye yaduma kulandela impumelelo kwi-1930s yemicu kunye neencwadi ezinje nge-The Adventures of Tintin. Iicomics zaseMelika zavela njengesixhobo esikhulu ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20 ngokufika kwamaphephandaba ahlekisayo; Iincwadi ezihlekisayo zohlobo lwamaphephancwadi zalandelwa ngeminyaka yee-1930, yaye uhlobo lwamaqhawe abalaseleyo lwaduma emva kokuvela kukaSuperman ngowe-1938. Amabali ahlekisayo aseJapan abanjwa ngokubanzi ngokwahlukileyo kwindaleko yamabali ahlekisayo e-Euro-American, kwaye ubugcisa bama-comic baseNtshona mhlawumbi bavela kwi-Itali yenkulungwane ye-17. Imicu yanamhlanje ehlekisayo yaseJapan yavela ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, kwaye imveliso yeemagazini ezihlekisayo kunye neencwadi zanda ngokukhawuleza emva kweMfazwe yeHlabathi yesiBini (1945)- ngokuthandwa kwabazobi abanjengo-Osamu Tezuka. I-Comics inegama eliphantsi kwimbali yayo eninzi, kodwa ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yama-20, yaqala ukufumana ukwamkelwa okukhulu kuluntu kunye nabafundi. 

Igama lesiNgesi elithi comics lisetyenziswa njengesibizo esikwisinye xa lisingisele kumxholo ngokwawo (umz. "IiKhomikhi luhlobo lobugcisa obubonwayo."), kodwa njengesininzi xa kubhekiswa kwimisebenzi edibeneyo (umz. "IiKhomikhi zizixhobo zokufunda ezithandwayo.").
