Incwadi yinkcazo ecwangcisiweyo yolwazi olurekhodiweyo, ubukhulu becala ngomlomo nangomzobo, kusetyenziswa isixhobo. Ekuqaleni, iincwadi ze-elektroniki kunye ne-audiobook zikhona ngoku. Iincwadi eziphathekayo zizinto eziqulethe imathiriyeli eshicilelweyo, ubukhulu becala obubhaliweyo nemifanekiso. Iincwadi zanamhlanje ngokuqhelekileyo ziyilwe ngamaphepha amaninzi adityanisiweyo aze akhuselwe ngeqweqwe, oko kwaziwa ngokuba yicodex format; iifomati ezindala ziquka umqulu kunye nethebhulethi. 
I-Etymology
 
Njengento yokucinga, incwadi ihlala ibhekisa kumsebenzi obhaliweyo wobude obuninzi ngombhali omnye okanye ngaphezulu, enokuthi isasazwe ngedijithali njengencwadi ye-elektroniki (ebook). Ezi ndidi zemisebenzi zinokuhlelwa ngokubanzi zibe yintsomi (equlathe umxholo oyiliweyo, amaxesha amaninzi amabali) nezingeyonyani (eziqulathe umxholo ojoliswe njengenyaniso eyinyani). Kodwa incwadi ebonakalayo ayinakuqulatha umsebenzi obhaliweyo: umzekelo, inokuba nemizobo kuphela, imizobo, iifoto, umculo wamaphepha, iipuzzle, okanye umxholo okhutshwayo njengoonodoli bephepha. 

Ishishini leencwadi langoku libone utshintsho olukhulu oluninzi ngenxa yetekhnoloji entsha, kubandakanya ii-ebooks kunye neaudiobooks (ukurekhoda kweencwadi ezifundwa ngokuvakalayo).Ukuqonda iimfuno zabantu abakhubazekileyo abashicilelweyo kukhokelele ekunyukeni kweefomathi ezenzelwe ukufikeleleka okukhulu okufana noshicilelo lwebraille kunye noshicilelo olukhulu.

Iincwadi zikaGoogle ziqikelelwa ngo-2010 ukuba malunga ne-130 yezigidi zeencwadi ezizodwa ziye zapapashwa. Inkqubo yokupapasha incwadi luluhlu lwamanyathelo abandakanyekayo ekudaleni nasekusasazeni iincwadi. Iincwadi zithengiswa kuzo zombini iivenkile eziqhelekileyo nakwiivenkile zeencwadi ezikhethekileyo, kunye nakwi-intanethi (ukuhanjiswa), kwaye zinokubolekwa kwiilayibrari okanye kwiikhabhathi zoluntu. Ukwamkelwa kweencwadi kukhokelele kwinani leziphumo zentlalo, kubandakanywa nokuhlolwa. 

Maxa wambi iincwadi zithelekiswa noncwadi lwamaxesha athile, olunjengamaphephandaba okanye amaphephancwadi, apho iinkupho ezintsha zipapashwa ngokocwangciso oluthe rhoqo. Izinto eziyeleleneyo, ezikwahlulahlulwe ngokubanzi “njengeencwadi”, zishiywa zingenanto ukuze zisetyenziswe buqu: njengakwimeko yeencwadi ze-akhawunti, iincwadi zokuqeshwa, iincwadi ze-autograph, iincwadi zamanqaku, iidayari kunye ne-sketchbook. 

Igama elithi incwadi livela kwi-Old English bōc, ekusenokwenzeka ukuba ivela kwingcambu yesiJamani *bōk-, ehambelana ne "beech".[1] Kwiilwimi zeSlavic ezifana nesiRashiya, isiBulgaria, isiMacedonian буква bukva—"ileta" ihambelana ne "beech". NgesiRashiya, isiSerbia kunye nesiMacedonian, igama elithi букварь (bukvar') okanye буквар (bukvar) libhekiselele kwincwadi yesikolo samabanga aphantsi enceda abantwana abancinci bakwazi ubuchule bokufunda nokubhala. Ngoko ke kucingelwa ukuba imibhalo yokuqala yase-Indo-European inokuba yakrolwa kwiplanga le-beech.[2] Igama lesiLatini elithi codex, elithetha incwadi ngokwengqiqo yanamhlanje (ebotshwe namagqabi ahlukeneyo), ntlandlolo lalithetha “ibhloko yomthi”.[3] 

Umfundi okhutheleyo okanye umqokeleli weencwadi yibhayibhiliyophile, okanye ngokwencoko "ngumbungu weencwadi".[4] 

Iingcaciso 
Ekubhalweni kwayo kwale mihla, incwadi idla ngokuqulunqwa ngamaphepha amaninzi (ahlala ephepheni, enziwe ngesikhumba, okanye enziwe ngesikhumba) adityaniswe kunye ecaleni elinye aze akhuselwe ngeqweqwe. Ngokwandiswa, incwadi ibhekisa kwincwadi ebonakalayo ebhaliweyo, eprintiweyo, okanye imizobo [5] Inxalenye enye okanye icandelo elinye lomsebenzi obhaliweyo omde lisenokubizwa ngokuba yincwadi, ngakumbi kwimisebenzi ethile eyaqanjwa mandulo: inxalenye nganye yeFiziksi ka-Aristotle, ngokomzekelo, yincwadi.[6] 

Kunzima ukwenza ingcaciso echanekileyo yencwadi eyichaza ngokucacileyo ukusuka kwezinye iindidi zezinto ezibhaliweyo kwixesha kunye nenkcubeko. Intsingiselo yeli gama itshintshile kakhulu ngokuhamba kwexesha ngokuvela kwamajelo onxibelelwano.[7] Umbhali-mbali weencwadi uJames Raven uye wacebisa ukuba xa kufundwa indlela iincwadi eziye zasetyenziswa ngayo ukunxibelelana, kufuneka zichazwe ngendlela ebandakanya ngokubanzi njengeendlela "eziphathwayo, ezihlala zihleli, eziphindiweyo nezifundekayo" zokurekhoda nokusasaza ulwazi, kunokuxhomekeka kwizinto ezibonakalayo okanye ezingokomxholo. Oku kuya kubandakanya, umzekelo, ii-ebooks, amaphephandaba, kunye nequipus (uhlobo loshicilelo olusekwe kwiqhina ngokwembali olwalusetyenziswa ziinkcubeko kwiAndean yaseMzantsi Melika), kodwa hayi izinto ezimisiweyo endaweni ezifana nezikhumbuzo ezibhaliweyo.[8][9]
 
Inkcazo engqongqo inikwa yi-UNESCO: ngeenjongo zokurekhoda iinkcukacha-manani zesizwe malunga nokuveliswa kweencwadi, iye yacebisa ukuba incwadi ichazwe “njengopapasho olungeyonxalenye yamaxesha athile olushicilelweyo ubuncinane lwamaphepha angama-49, ngaphandle kwamaphepha angaphandle, apapashiweyo kweli lizwe aze afumaneke kuluntu”, ezahlula kwezinye izinto ezibhaliweyo ezifana namaphecana.[5][10] Kovač et al. bayihlabile le ngcaciso ngokusilela ukunika ingxelo kwiifomati zedijithali ezintsha. Bacebisa iikhrayitheriya ezine (ubude obuncinane; umxholo wombhalo; ifom enemida echaziweyo; kunye "nolwakhiwo lolwazi" njengesakhiwo somgca kunye nezinto ezithile zombhalo) ezenza "uluhlu lwencwadi", apho iifomathi ezizalisekisa iinqobo ezingakumbi zijongwa ngokufana ngakumbi nencwadi yemveli eshicilelweyo.[11][12]
 
Nangona kulwimi lwezemfundo imonograph ingumsebenzi oyincutshe kwisifundo esinye, kwithala leencwadi nakwinzululwazi yolwazi eli gama lisetyenziswa ngokubanzi ukuthetha naluphi na ushicilelo olungalandelelaniyo olugqityiweyo kumqulu omnye (incwadi ebonakalayo) okanye inani eliqinisekileyo lemiqulu (enjengenoveli enemiqulu emininzi), ngokuchaseneyo noshicilelo olulandelelanayo okanye lwamaxesha athile.[13][6] 

Imbali 
Inqaku eliphambili: Imbali yeencwadi 

Umphambili ontsonkothileyo weDiamond Sutra evela kumnombo waseTang eTshayina, okt 868 CE, eyona ncwadi indala eyaziwayo eshicilelweyo ehlabathini (iThala leeNcwadi laseBritani) 
Imbali yeencwadi yaba luqeqesho oluvunyiweyo lwezemfundo ngeminyaka yee-1980. Igalelo kweli candelo livela kwizifundo zokubhaliweyo, icodicology, ibhibliyografi, iphilology, ipalaeography, imbali yobugcisa, imbali yezentlalo kunye nembali yenkcubeko. Ijonge ukubonisa ukuba incwadi njengento, hayi nje isicatshulwa esiqulethwe kuyo, ngumjelo wokusebenzisana phakathi kwabafundi namagama. Uhlalutyo lwecandelo ngalinye lencwadi lunokutyhila injongo yayo, apho yayigcinwe khona kwaye njani, ifundwe ngubani na, iinkolelo ezingokwembono nezenkolo zelo xesha, nokuba abafundi banxibelelane kusini na nesicatshulwa ngaphakathi. Kwanokunqongophala kobungqina obunjalo kunokushiya imikhondo ebalulekileyo malunga nohlobo lwencwadi ethile. 

Iindlela zokuqala zokubhala zazikrolwa kumacwecwe, eguqulelwa ekubeni ngamagqabi esundu nakumpapiri kumaxesha amandulo. I-Parchment kunye nephepha kamva zavela njenge-substrates ebalulekileyo yokwenza incwadi, ukwazisa ukuqina okukhulu kunye nokufikeleleka.[14] Kuyo yonke imimandla efana neTshayina, uMbindi Mpuma, iYurophu, noMzantsi Asia, kwavela iindlela ezahlukeneyo zokuvelisa iincwadi. AmaXesha Aphakathi wabona ukuvela kwemibhalo-ngqangi ekhanyisiweyo, edibanisa ngokuntsonkothileyo umbhalo kunye nemifanekiso, ngakumbi ngexesha leMughal eMzantsi Asia phantsi kwenkxaso yabalawuli abafana no-Akbar kunye no-Shah Jahan.[15][16]

Ngaphambi kokuveliswa komatshini wokushicilela ngenkulungwane ye-15, owathi waduma yiBhayibhile kaGutenberg, umbhalo ngamnye wawulinqaku elixabisekileyo elenziwe ngesandla, elenzelwe umntu ngamnye ngokweenkalo zoyilo ezidityaniswe ngumbhali, umnini, umbhidi weencwadi nomzobi wemifanekiso.[17] Ukwenziwa kwayo kuphawule umzuzu obalulekileyo wokuveliswa kweencwadi. Iinguqulelo ezintsha ezifana nohlobo olushukumayo kunye noomatshini bokushicilela abaqhutywa ngumphunga zikhawulezise iinkqubo zokwenziwa kwemveliso kwaye zibe negalelo ekwandeni kwamazinga okufunda nokubhala. Ukhuseleko lwelungelo lokushicilela luye lwavela, lukhusela amalungelo ababhali kunye nokubumba imbonakalo yokushicilela.[18] IXesha laMva laMava lazisa iincwadi zeencwadi, ezilungiselela uluhlu olubanzi lwabafundi, kunye nokwenziwa kwenkqubo yoshicilelo ngoomatshini kuphucule ngakumbi ukusebenza kakuhle. 

Ngenkulungwane yama-20 kuye kwavela oomatshini bokuchwetheza, iikhompyutha, noshicilelo lwedesktop, beguqula ukwenziwa kwamaxwebhu nokushicilela. Inkqubela phambili yedijithali kwinkulungwane yama-21 ikhokelele ekunyukeni kweencwadi ze-ebooks, eziphenjelelwa kudumo lwabafundayo kunye neempawu zokufikeleleka. Ngelixa iingxoxo malunga nokuhla okunokubakho kweencwadi zenyama ziye zavela, imidiya yoshicilelo ibonakalise ukomelela ngokumangalisayo, iqhubeka ikhula njengeshishini leebhiliyoni zeedola.[19] Ukongezelela, iinzame zokwenza uncwadi lubandakanyeke ngakumbi luye lwavela, ngokuphuhliswa kweBraille yabantu abangaboniyo kunye nokuyilwa kweencwadi ezithethwayo, kulungiselelwa iindlela ezizezinye zokuba abantu bafikelele kwaye banandiphe uncwadi.[20] 


Iziqwenga zeMiyalelo yeShuruppak, yasekuqaleni kwe-3rd millennium BC 
Ithebhulethi  
aphambili: Ithebhulethi yodongwe kunye nethebhulethi yeWax
Ezinye zeerekhodi ezibhaliweyo zokuqala zenziwe kwiipilisi. Amacwecwe odongwe (iingceba zodongwe ezisicaba ezichotywe ngosiba) zazisetyenziswa kwiMpuma Ekufuphi naMandulo kulo lonke ixesha leBronze Age ukuya kutsho nakwi-Iron Age, ingakumbi ekubhaleni ngoonobumba abatsobhileyo. Iipilisi ze-wax (iziqwenga zokhuni ezigqunywe kuluhlu lwe-wax) zazisetyenziswa kwi-classical yakudala kunye nakwi-Middle Ages. 

Isiko lokubopha amacwecwe e-wax aliqela kunye (i-Roman pugillares) ngumanduleli onokwenzeka weencwadi zale mihla.[21] Imvelaphi yegama elithi codex (ibloko lomthi) libonisa ukuba lisenokuba laphuhliswa kumacwecwe enziwe ngamaplanga.[22] 

Skrola 
Inqaku eliphambili: 

Incwadi Yomsongo yabafileyo baseHunefer; c. 1275 BC; i-inki kunye ne-pigments kwi-papyrus; 45 × 90.5 cm; IMyuziyam yaseBritane (eLondon) 
Imisongo eyenziwe ngepapyrus yaqala ukusetyenziselwa ukubhalwa kwi-Egypt yaMandulo, mhlawumbi kwangexesha loLawulo lokuQala, nangona ubungqina bamandulo buphuma kwiincwadi ze-akhawunti zikaKumkani uNeferirkare Kakai weSihlanu Sobukhosi (malunga nama-2400 BC). NgokukaHerodotus (Imbali 5:58), amaFenike azisa umbhalo kunye nompapiri eGrisi malunga nenkulungwane ye-10 okanye ye-9 BC. Enoba yayisenziwa ngompapiri, ngesikhumba, okanye ngephepha, imisongo yayiyeyona ndlela ibalaseleyo yokubhala kwizithethe zamaGrike, zamaRoma, zamaTshayina, isiHebhere nezaseMakedoni. Incwadi yamandulo yayigquba kwimida yamaRoma, kodwa imisongo yayikho ixesha elide eAsiya.
 
Codex 
Inqaku eliphambili: 

Iincwadi zeCodex Chinese bamboo zidibana nengcaciso yale mihla yecodex. Le ncwadi ye-bamboo yikopi ye-Sun Tzu yobuGcisa beMfazwe. 
Icodex ngunozala wencwadi yanamhlanje, equlathe amaphepha anobukhulu obufanayo adityaniswe ecaleni kwelinye kwaye abanjwa phakathi kwamaqweqwe amabini enziwe ngemathiriyeli eyomeleleyo. U-Isidore waseSeville (wafa ngo-636) wachaza ulwalamano lwangoku phakathi kwe-codex, incwadi, kunye nomsongo kwi-Etymologiae (VI.13) yakhe: "I-codex yenziwe ngeencwadi ezininzi; incwadi yencwadi enye. Ibizwa ngokuba yi-codex ngendlela yomzekeliso ovela kwiziqu (codex) yemithi okanye i-stocks, njengokuba iqulethwe kwi-stock, njengokuba iqulethwe yimithi okanye imidiliya. babengamasebe". 

Incwadi yokuqala ekhankanyiweyo yecodex njengohlobo oluthile lwencwadi ivela kuMartial, kwincwadi yakhe ethi Apophoreta CLXXXIV ekupheleni kwenkulungwane yokuqala, apho akuncoma ukucutheka kwayo. Noko ke, le codex ayizange ifumane ukuthandwa kakhulu kwihlabathi lobuhedeni lobuGrike, yaye kuphela kubuKristu apho yathi yasetyenziswa ngokubanzi.[23] Olu tshintsho lwenzeka ngokuthe ngcembe ebudeni benkulungwane yesi-3 neyesi-4, yaye izizathu zokwamkela uhlobo lwe<em>codex yale ncwadi zaziliqela: indlela eyayibhalwe ngayo yayiyonga ngakumbi kunomsongo, njengoko kunokusetyenziswa macala omabini ombandela; kwaye yayiphatheka, ikhangeleke, kwaye kulula ukuyifihla. Ababhali abangamaKristu basenokuba babefuna ukwahlula imibhalo yabo kwimibhalo yobuhedeni neyamaYuda eyayibhalwe kwimisongo. 

Iikhowudi ze-pre-Columbian Mesoamerica zazinefomu efanayo ne-European codex, kodwa endaweni yoko zenziwe ngemicu emide esongiweyo nokuba yeyiphi na ixolo lomkhiwane (amatl) okanye imicu yezityalo, rhoqo inomaleko we-whitewash efakwa phambi kokubhala. Iikhowudi zehlabathi elitsha zabhalwa kwangenkulungwane ye-16 (jonga iikhowudi zamaMaya kunye neekhowudi zama-Aztec). Ezo zibhalwe ngaphambi koloyiso lwaseSpain zibonakala ngathi zonke zingamashiti amade asongwe ngendlela yekonsathi, ngamanye amaxesha ebhalwe kumacala omabini ephepha le-amatl lasekhaya. 

Umbhalo-ngqangi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umbhalo-ngqangi 
Khangela kwakhona: Umbhalo-ngqangi wamagqabi esundu

IFolio 14 recto yenkulungwane ye-5 iVergilius Romanus iqulethe umfanekiso wombhali kaVirgil. Qaphela i-bookcase (capsa), indawo yokufunda kunye nesicatshulwa esibhaliweyo ngaphandle kwezithuba zamagama ngoonobumba abakhulu be-rustic.  
Imibhalo-ngqangi, amaxwebhu abhalwe ngesandla nakhutshelwe ngesandla, yayikuphela kwendlela yokubhala ngaphambi kokuveliswa nokwamkelwa ngokubanzi koshicilelo. Ukuqhubela phambili kwenziwa kwiindlela ezisetyenziselwa ukuyila.

Ekuqaleni koBukhosi bamaRoma aseNtshona, izindlu zoonongendi zaqhubeka nezithethe zokubhalwa kwesiLatini eziphathelele ubuKristu, yaye abefundisi ngabona baninzi bafunda nabakhupheli. Inkqubo yokwenza incwadi yayinde kwaye inzima. Ayedla ngokubhalwa kwisikhumba okanye kwivellum, kubhalwe kumphezulu owenziwe ngesikhumba sesilwanyana esilungisiweyo. Iphepha lesikhumba kwakufuneka lilungiswe, emva koko amaphepha angadityaniswanga acwangciswe aze alawulwe ngesixhobo esibuthuntu okanye ilothe, emva koko umbhalo ubhalwe ngumbhali, owayedla ngokushiya iindawo ezingabhalwanga ukuze zifanekisele yaye zixutywe. Ekugqibeleni, yayibotshelelwa ngumdibi weencwadi.[24] 

Ngenxa yobunzima obubandakanyekileyo ekwenzeni nasekukhupheleni iincwadi, zazibiza yaye zinqabile. Izindlu zoonongendi ezincinci zazidla ngokuba neencwadi nje ezimbalwa. Ngenkulungwane yesi-9, ingqokelela enkulu yabanjwa malunga nemithamo engama-500 kwaye nasekupheleni kweXesha Eliphakathi, ithala leencwadi likapopu eAvignon naseParis kwithala leencwadi laseSorbonne laliphethe imiqulu engama-2,000 kuphela. 

Ukwanda kweeyunivesithi ngenkulungwane ye-13 kwabangela ukuba kufuneke iincwadi ezininzi, yaye kwavela inkqubo entsha yokukhuphela. Ezi ncwadi zazahlulwa zaba ngamagqabi angadityaniswanga ( pecia ), awayebolekiswa kubakhupheli abahlukahlukeneyo, ngoko isantya sokwenziwa kweencwadi sakhula ngokuphawulekayo. Le nkqubo yagcinwa yimibutho yehlabathi yamagosa osasazo, eyavelisa izinto ezizezonqulo nezingezizo ezenkolo.[26] 


Umbhali nombhali waseBurgundi uJean Miélot, ophuma kwiMimangaliso yakhe ye-Notre Dame, kwinkulungwane ye-15 
EIndiya, imibhalo-ngqangi ebotshelelweyo eyenziwe ngexolo lebhirch okanye amagqabi esundu yayikho ukususela mandulo.[27] Umbhalo okwimibhalo-ngqangi yamagqabi esundu wawubhalwe ngosiba lwemela kuxwebhu olusikiwe oluxande kunye namagqabi esundu acoliweyo; Umbala wawuqatywa kumphezulu uze wosule, ushiya i-inki kwimikrozo ekroliweyo. Iphepha ngalinye lalinomngxuma ekunokudlula kuwo umtya, yaye ngawo amaphepha ayedityaniswa ngomtya ukuze abophe okwencwadi. 

I-Woodblock printing 

Bagh print, indlela yoshicilelo yeplanga yemveli eyavela eBagh, eMadhya Pradesh, eIndiya 
Inqaku eliphambili:
Kushicilelo lweplanga, umfanekiso okroliweyo wephepha lonke ukrolwa kwiibhloko zomthi, inki, uze usetyenziswe ukuprinta iikopi zelo phepha. Yavela kwinzala kaHan ngaphambi kowama-220 AD, yayisetyenziselwa ukuprinta amalaphu kunye nephepha kamva, kwaye yayisetyenziswa kakhulu kulo lonke elaseMpuma Asia. Eyona ncwadi indala yomhla eprintwe yile ndlela yiThe Diamond Sutra (868 AD). Indlela (ebizwa ngokuba yiplanga xa isetyenziswa kubugcisa) yafika eYurophu ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-14. Iincwadi (ezaziwa ngokuba zii-block-books), kunye namakhadi okudlala nemifanekiso yonqulo, zaqalisa ukuveliswa ngale ndlela. Ukuyila incwadi epheleleyo kwakuyinkqubo enzima, efuna ibhloko eqingqwe ngesandla kwiphepha ngalinye, yaye iibhloko zomthi zazinokuqhekeka ukuba zigcinwe ixesha elide. 

Uhlobo olushenxisekayo kunye ne-incunabula  
Amanqaku aphambili: Uhlobo olushukumayo kunye ne-Incunable

Iimfundiso Ezikhethiweyo ZeeNgcali zamaBhuda neeNgcweti zoNyana, eyona ncwadi yakudala eyaziwayo eyashicilelwa ngodidi lwesinyithi olushukumayo, eyashicilelwa eKorea, ngowe-1377, iBibliothèque nationale de France 
Umqambi waseTshayina uBi Sheng wenza uhlobo olunokushenxiswa lwezitya zodongwe c. 1045, kodwa akukho mizekelo yaziwayo yokushicilela kwakhe. Malunga ne-1450, uJohannes Gutenberg waqamba ngokuzimeleyo uhlobo olushukumayo eYurophu, kunye nezinto ezintsha zokuyila uhlobo olusekwe kwimatrix kunye nokungunda ngesandla. Oku kuyilwa ngokuthe ngcembe kwenza iincwadi zangabizi mali ininzi ukuzivelisa zaza zafumaneka ngokubanzi. Iincwadi zokuqala ezishicilelweyo, amaphepha angatshatanga kunye nemifanekiso eyadalwa ngaphambi ko-1501 eYurophu zaziwa njengezinto ezingenakukwazi ukunyanyiswa okanye ezifakwe kwi-incunabula.[28] 


Inkulungwane ye-15 Engenakufezekiswa 
yenkulungwane ye-19 yokubonisa 
oomatshini bokushicilela abaqhutywa ngumphunga baye baduma ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19. Aba matshini babekwazi ukushicilela amaphepha ali-1,100 ngeyure,[29] kodwa abasebenzi babenokuseta kuphela oonobumba abangama-2,000 ngeyure.[icatshulwa] Oomatshini bokuchwetheza beMonotype kunye nelinotype baqaliswa ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19. Babenokuseta oonobumba abangaphezu kwama-6 000 ngeyure kunye nomgca opheleleyo wohlobo ngaxeshanye. Kuye kwakho uphuculo oluninzi kumatshini wokushicilela. Phakathi kwinkulungwane yama-20, ukuveliswa kweencwadi eYurophu kuye kwantinga ukuya kutsho ngaphezu kwezihloko ezingama-200 000 ngonyaka. 

Ebudeni benkulungwane yama-20, amathala eencwadi ebesoloko ekhula, maxa wambi ebizwa ngokuba kukwanda kwenkcazelo. Ukufika kokupapashwa kwe-elektroniki kunye ne-intanethi kuthetha ukuba ulwazi olutsha luhlala lupapashwa kwi-intanethi kuneencwadi eziprintiweyo, umzekelo ngelayibrari yedijithali. "Shicilela ngokufunwayo" ubuchwepheshe, okwenza kube lula ukuprinta nje ezimbalwa njengencwadi enye ngexesha, zenze ukuzipapasha (kunye nopapasho lwamampunge) kube lula kwaye kufikeleleke ngakumbi, kwaye kuvumele abapapashi ukuba bagcine iincwadi ezithengiswa kancinci ziprintwe kunokuba zibhengeze ukuba aziprintwa. 

Upapasho lwangoku 
Inqaku eliphambili: Upapasho
Okwangoku, iincwadi ziveliswa yinkampani epapashayo ukuze zibekwe emarikeni ngabasasazi kunye neevenkile ezithengisa iincwadi. Umpapashi uthethathethana ngesivumelwano esisemthethweni esisemthethweni kunye nababhali ukuze bafumane ilungelo lokushicilela imisebenzi, emva koko balungiselele ukuba ziveliswe kwaye zithengiswe. Awona manyathelo aphambili enkqubo yokupapasha ngala: ukuhlela nokufunda umsebenzi oza kupapashwa; ukuyila incwadi eprintiweyo; ukwenza iincwadi; kunye nokuthengisa iincwadi, kubandakanywa ukuthengisa kunye nokukhuthaza. Inyathelo ngalinye kula lidla ngokuthathwa ziinkampani zangaphandle ezihlawulwa ngumpapashi.[30] Oku kuchasene nokuzipapasha, apho umbhali ehlawulela ukuveliswa kunye nokuhanjiswa komsebenzi wabo kwaye alawule amanye okanye onke amanyathelo enkqubo yokupapasha.[31] 

Ukupapasha ngolwimi lwesiNgesi okwangoku kulawulwa ngabo babizwa ngokuba yi "Big Five" abapapashi: iPenguin Random House, iHachette Book Group, iHarperCollins, uSimon & Schuster, kunye noMacmillan Publishers. Baqikelelwa ukuba benze phantse i-60 yepesenti yemarike yeencwadi zokufunda ngokubanzi ngo-2021. [32] 

Uyilo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Uyilo lwencwadi 
Uyilo lwencwadi bubugcisa bokubandakanya umxholo, isimbo, ifomathi, uyilo, kunye nolandelelwano lwezinto ezahlukeneyo zencwadi kwiyunithi ehambelanayo.[33] 

Ubeko 
Bona kwakhona: Uyilo lwephepha 


Umzobo wencwadi 
Ibhendi yeBelly 
Flap 
Iphepha Lokugqibela 
Cover 
Head 
Fore edge 
Umsila 
Iphepha lasekunene (recto ukuba ushicilelo lukhohlo ukuya ekunene, verso ukuba ekunene ukuya ekhohlo) 
Iphepha lasekhohlo (verso ukuba ushicilelo lushiywe ukuya ekunene, recto ukuba ekunene ukuya ekhohlo 
)
Iincwadi zale mihla zicwangciswa ngokwendlela ethile ebizwa ngokuba yisakhiwo sencwadi. Nangona kukho umahluko omkhulu kuyilo, iincwadi zanamhlanje zikholisa ukubambelela kuluhlu lwemithetho malunga nokuba zeziphi iinxalenye zoyilo kunye nokuba umxholo wazo udla ngokubandakanya ntoni. Uyilo olusisiseko luya kubandakanya iqweqwe langaphambili, iqweqwe elingasemva kunye nomxholo wencwadi obizwa ngokuba yikopi yomzimba wayo okanye amaphepha omxholo. Iqweqwe elingaphambili lidla ngokuba nesihloko sencwadi (kunye nesihlokwana, ukuba sikhona) kunye negama lombhali okanye umhleli (abahleli). Iphepha elingaphakathi elingaphandle lidla ngokushiywa lingenanto kuzo zombini iincwadi ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni kunye nephepha. Icandelo elilandelayo, ukuba likhona, ngumbandela ophambili wencwadi, oquka zonke izinto ezibhaliweyo emva kweqweqwe langaphambili kodwa ingeyiyo inxalenye yomxholo wencwadi njengentshayelelo, unikezelo, uluhlu lwemixholo kunye nedatha yompapashi efana noshicilelo lwencwadi okanye inombolo yokushicilela kunye nendawo yokushicilela. Phakathi kwekopi yomzimba kunye neqweqwe elingasemva liya kumcimbi wokugqibela oya kubandakanya naziphi na izalathisi, iiseti zeetheyibhile, imizobo, iiglosari okanye uluhlu lwemisebenzi ecatshulweyo (nangona incwadi ehleliweyo enababhali abaliqela idla ngokubeka imisebenzi ecatshulweyo ekupheleni kwesahluko ngasinye esigunyazisiweyo). Iphepha elingaphakathi elingasemva, elifana nelingaphakathi kwikhava yangaphambili, lidla ngokuba lingenanto. Iqweqwe elingasemva yindawo yesiqhelo ye-ISBN yencwadi kwaye mhlawumbi ifoto yombhali(aba)/ umhleli(aba), mhlawumbi ngentshayelelo emfutshane kubo. Kwakhona apha kudla ngokuvela isishwankathelo sebali, iibhakhowudi kunye nophononongo olucatshulweyo lwencwadi.[34] 

Umzimba weencwadi udla ngokwahlulwa ube ngamacandelo, izahluko, amacandelo kwaye ngamanye amaxesha amacandelwana aqulunqwe ubuncinane ngumhlathi okanye ngaphezulu. 
 
Ubungakanani 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ubungakanani bencwadi
Ubukhulu bencwadi ngokuqhelekileyo bulinganiswa ngobude nobubanzi begqabi, okanye maxa wambi ubude nobubanzi beqweqwe layo.[35] Uthotho lwamagama adla ngokusetyenziswa ngamathala eencwadi anamhlanje kunye nabapapashi kwiisayizi ngokubanzi zeencwadi zale mihla ukusuka kwifolio (elikhulu), ukuya kwiquarto (encinci) kunye ne-octavo (esencinci). Ngokomlando, la magama abhekiselele kwifomathi yencwadi, igama lobugcisa elisetyenziswa ngabashicileli kunye nababhali bebhayibhilografi ukubonisa ubungakanani begqabi ngokobungakanani bephepha lokuqala. Umzekelo, iquarto yayiyincwadi eprintwe kumaphepha asongwe kabini, ize elokuqala ligotywe likwiengile ezichanekileyo ukuya kwelesibini, ukuze livelise amagqabi ama-4 (okanye amaphepha asi-8), igqabi ngalinye libe linye ngokwesine ubukhulu bephepha lokuqala elishicilelweyo – qaphela ukuba igqabi libhekisela kwisiqwenga sephepha esinye, ngoxa iphepha likwicala elinye legqabi. Ngenxa yokuba eyona ndlela yokubhalwa kweencwadi zanamhlanje ingenakuqondwa xa kuhlolisiswa iincwadi, ababhali beBhayibhile basenokungawasebenzisi la magama kwiinkcazelo zabaphengululi. 

Umzobo 
Inqaku eliphambili: 
Umzekeliso wencwadi obonisa umqhagi okhalayo ujonge ilanga liphuma nendoda, enxibe i-nightcap kunye nempahla yokulala, yoyame ngefestile. Imvelaphi ibonisa abantu ababini abancinci abahamba kwindlela ebiyelweyo.
Umzobo ovela "kwiNdlu eyakhiwa nguJack" kwiNgqokelela eGqibeleleyo yeMifanekiso & neeNgoma; ukukrola kunye noshicilelo ngu-Edmund Evans, umzobo kaRandolph Caldecott (1887) 
Nangona uhlobo oluthile lomfanekiso wencwadi lukho ukususela ekuyilweni kokubhalwa, isithethe sanamhlanje semizekeliso saseNtshona saqala ngeencwadi zebhloko zenkulungwane ye-15, apho isicatshulwa sencwadi kunye nemifanekiso yasikwa kwibhloko enye.[36] Ubuchwephesha obufana nokukrola, ukukrolwa, kunye ne-lithography nazo zibe nefuthe. 

Ukwenziwa kweencwadi 

ezininzi ezijikelezayo eziboniswe kwishelufu 
Iindlela ezisetyenziselwa ukuprinta kunye nokudityaniswa kweencwadi zaqhubeka zingatshintshwanga ukusuka kwinkulungwane ye-15 ukuya ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yama-20. Ngoxa kwakukho oomatshini abangakumbi, ngowe-1900 umshicileli weencwadi wayesasebenzisa uhlobo lwesinyithi olushukumayo oludityaniswe ngamagama, imigca namaphepha ukwenza imibhalo. Iincwadi zamaphepha zangoku ziprintwa ephepheni elenzelwe ngokukodwa ukuprinta. Ngokwemveli, amaphepha eencwadi anamaphepha amhlophe-mhlophe okanye amhlophe aphantsi (afundeka lula), acwebile ukunciphisa umboniso wombhalo ukusuka kwelinye icala lephepha ukuya kwelinye kwaye (ngokuqhelekileyo) enziwa ukuba abe ngqongqo okanye angqingqwa, ngakumbi kwiincwadi ezibophelelekileyo. Iimpawu zephepha ezahlukeneyo zisetyenziswa ngokuxhomekeke kuhlobo lwencwadi: Umatshini ogqityiweyo wamaphepha agqunywe, amaphepha angagqunywanga ngamaplanga, amaphepha agqunyiweyo kunye namaphepha acolekileyo akhethekileyo ngamabakala ephepha aqhelekileyo. 

 
Inoveli yowe-1870 ethi The Seven Brothers ka-Aleksis Kivi yaqala ukupapashwa ngemiqulu emine emifutshane.
Namhlanje, uninzi lweencwadi ziprintwa nge-offset lithography.[37] Xa incwadi iprintwa, amaphepha abekwa epleyitini ukuze emva kokuba iphepha elishicilelweyo lilisongwe amaphepha abe ngolandelelwano oluchanekileyo. Iincwadi zidla ngokuveliswa namhlanje ngokwemilinganiselo embalwa eqhelekileyo. Iisayizi zeencwadi zidla ngokuchazwa njenge "trim size": ubungakanani bephepha emva kokuba iphepha lisongiwe kwaye lilungiswe. Ubungakanani obuqhelekileyo buvela kubungakanani bamaphepha (ngoko ke oomatshini bobukhulu) abathe baduma kwiminyaka engama-200 okanye engama-300 eyadlulayo, kwaye beza kulawula ishishini. Iindibano zaseBritani kulo mba zikho kulo lonke ilizwe labantetho isisiNgesi, ngaphandle kwase-US. Ishishini lokwenziwa kweencwadi laseYurophu lisebenza kumgangatho owahluke ngokupheleleyo. 

Iincwadi ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni zibophene ngokuqinileyo, ngoxa iincwadi ezinoqweqwe olulukhuni zinamaqweqwe angabizi kakhulu, abhetyebhetye adla ngokungonakali ixesha elide. Abapapashi banokuvelisa iikopi ezipapashiweyo ezinexabiso eliphantsi ezaziwa ngokuba zii-galleys okanye "bonding proofs" ngeenjongo zokwazisa, ezifana nokwenza uphononongo kwangaphambi kokupapashwa. Iinqanawa zeenqwelo-moya zidla ngokwenziwa ngexabiso eliphantsi kangangoko kunokwenzeka, ekubeni zingenzelwanga kuthengiswa. 

Ushicilelo 

Eli candelo lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo lokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Februwari 2024) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo)
Ezinye iincwadi, ngakumbi ezo zinemiba emifutshane (okt ezineekopi ezimbalwa) ziya kuprintwa koomatshini bokushicilela be-sheet-fed offset, kodwa uninzi lweencwadi ngoku ziprintwa koomatshini bokushicilela bewebhu, abondliwa ngoluhlu oluqhubekayo lwephepha, kwaye ngenxa yoko banokuprinta ezinye iikopi ngexesha elifutshane. Njengoko umgca wemveliso ujikeleza, "incwadi" epheleleyo iqokelelwa ndawonye kwi-stack yamaphepha, kwaye omnye umatshini uqhuba ukugoqa, ukuncenga, kunye nokuthungwa kwamaphepha kwiingxowa zesignesha (amacandelo amaphepha) alungele ukungena kumgca wokuqokelela. Amaphepha encwadi ashicilelwa kabini ngexesha, kungekhona njengencwadi enye epheleleyo. Amanani angaphezulu aprintwa ukwenza nakuphi na ukumoshwa ngenxa yokwenziwa kwezinto okanye amaphepha ovavanyo ukuqinisekisa umgangatho wokugqibela wokuprinta.
 
Ukuzilungisa ngumsebenzi wokulungiselela owenziwa ngoomatshini bokushicilela ukuze umatshini wokushicilela ufikelele kumgangatho ofunekayo wophawu. Okubandakanyiweyo ekuzilungiseleleni lixesha elithathiweyo ukunyusela ipleyiti kumatshini, ucoce nabuphi na ubumdaka obusuka kumsebenzi wangaphambili, kwaye unyuse ucinezelo ukuba ukhawuleze. Kwakamsinya nje akuba umshicileli egqibe kwelokuba ukuprinta kuchanekile, onke amaphepha asele enziwe umatshini aya kulahlwa, yaye umatshini wokushicilela uya kuqalisa ukwenza iincwadi. Ukwenza ukulungelelaniswa okufanayo kwenzeka kwiindawo zokugoqa kunye nokubopha, nganye ibandakanya ukuchithwa kwephepha.

Uphuhliso lwakutsha nje kwimveliso yeencwadi lubandakanya uphuhliso loshicilelo lwedijithali. Amaphepha eencwadi aprintwa, ngendlela efanayo naleyo esebenza ngayo umkhupheli weofisi, esebenzisa itoner kune-inki. Incwadi nganye iprintwa njengepasi elinye, kungekhona njengeesignitsha ezahlukeneyo. Ushicilelo lwedijithali luvumele ukwenziwa kwezinto ezincinci kune-offset, ngokuyinxenye ngenxa yokungabikho kokulungiswa kunye nokonakaliswa. Ukuprintwa kwedijithali kuye kwavula ithuba lokuprinta-kwimfuno, apho kungekho ncwadi ziprintwayo de kube semva kokuba iodolo ifunyenwe kumthengi. 


Iimitha ezili-12 ukuphakama (40 ft) umfanekiso oqingqiweyo wemfumba yeencwadi kwiBerlin Walk of Ideas, isikhumbuzo sokuyilwa koshicilelo lweencwadi lwale mihla 
Ukubophelela 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukudityaniswa kweencwadi 
Emva kokuba imisayino isongiwe kwaye iqokelelwe, baya kungena kwindawo yokudibanisa iincwadi. Embindini wenkulungwane edlulileyo kwakusekho izibophelelo ezininzi zokurhweba—iinkampani ezizibophelelayo zodwa ezingazange zishicilele, ezikhethekileyo ekuzibopheleleni zodwa. Ngelo xesha, ngenxa yokongamela kokushicilela ngoonobumba, ukusetwa nokushicilela kwakusenzeka kwindawo enye, kwaza kwadityaniswa kumzi-mveliso owahlukileyo. Xa udidi lwaluyintsimbi yonke, uhlobo lwexabiso lwencwadi eqhelekileyo lunokuba lukhulu, lubuthathaka kwaye lubenzima. Okukhona ishukunyiswa kancinane kule meko kokukhona bhetele: ngoko ukushicilela kwakuya kuqhutyelwa kwindawo enye nocwangciso lohlobo. Amaphepha ashicilelweyo kwelinye icala ayenokushukunyiswa lula. Ngoku, ngenxa yokwanda kokusetyenziswa kwekhompyutha ekulungiseleleni incwadi yomshicileli, inxenye yokuseta umsebenzi iye yanyuka yaya ngasentla, apho yenziwa khona mhlawumbi ziinkampani ezisebenzela umshicileli ngokwahlukeneyo, ngabapapashi ngokwabo, okanye ngababhali. Ukudityaniswa kweshishini lokwenziwa kweencwadi kuthetha ukuba ngoku akuqhelekanga ukufumana umdibaniso wokudibanisa iincwadi ongabandakanyekiyo nakushicilelo lweencwadi (kunye nangenye indlela). 

Ukuba incwadi ngumqolo onzima umendo wayo kwi-bindery iya kubandakanya amanqaku amaninzi omsebenzi kunokuba i-paperback. Ukubophelela okungafakwanga kuxhaphake ngoku. Izisayino zencwadi zinokubanjwa kunye "ngokuthunga okukaSmyth" kusetyenziswa iinaliti, "ukuthunga kweMcCain", kusetyenziswa imingxuma egrunjiweyo edla ngokusetyenziswa ekudibaneni kweencwadi zesikolo, okanye "i-notch binding", apho ukutyhutyha malunga ne-intshi ubude kwenziwa ngamaxesha athile ngokugotywa kumqolo wesiginitsha nganye. Eminye inkqubo yokubophelela iyafana kuzo zonke iimeko. Iincwadi ezithungelweyo kunye neenotshi zinokubotshwa njengee-hardbacks okanye ii-paperbacks. 

Ukugqiba 
"Ukwenza iimeko" kwenzeka ngaphandle kwe-intanethi kwaye ngaphambi kokufika kwencwadi kumgca wokubopha. Kweyona nto isisiseko sokwenza, iziqwenga ezibini zekhadibhodi zibekwe kwilaphu elincanyathisiweyo elinesithuba phakathi kwazo apho kufakwe ibhodi encancayo esikwe kububanzi bomqolo wencwadi. Imiphetho edibeneyo yelaphu (malunga ne-5/8" ngeenxa zonke) igoqwe phezu kweebhodi, kwaye icinezelwe ukuba ibambelele.Emva kokwenza i-stack yamatyala iya kwindawo ye-foil stamping yokongeza imihlobiso kunye nohlobo.
 
ukuthengisa kunye nokusasazwa 
kwenqaku eliphambili: 
Ukuthengiswa kweencwadi kurhwebo lweencwadi ezithi zenze isiphelo sokuthengisa kunye nokuhanjiswa kwenkqubo yokupapasha. 

Ushicilelo olufikelelekayo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ushicilelo olufikelelekayo 
Umzekelo womntu osebenzisa umfundi wesikrini obonisa amaxwebhu angenakufikeleleka, afundekayo kwaye afikeleleke 
Ukupapasha okufikelelekayo yindlela yokupapasha kunye noyilo lwencwadi apho iincwadi kunye nezinye izicatshulwa zenziwa zifumaneke kwiifomathi ezizezinye ezenzelwe ukunceda okanye ukubuyisela inkqubo yokufunda. Ibaluleke kakhulu kubantu abangaboniyo, abangaboniyo okanye abashicilelweyo. 

Ezinye iifomati eziye zaphuhliswa ukunceda abantu abohlukeneyo ukuba bafunde ziquka iindidi zeefonti ezinkulu, iifonti ezikhethekileyo zohlobo oluthile lokukhubazeka kokufunda, i-braille, ii-ebooks, kunye ne-audiobooks ezenzekelayo kunye ne-DAISY yedijithali ethetha iincwadi. 

Upapasho olufikelelekayo lwenziwe lula ngophuhliso lwetekhnoloji efana nokuprintwa ngokwemfuno, abafundi be-ebook, ifomathi yedatha ecwangcisiweyo ye-XML, ifomathi ye-EPUB3 kunye ne-Intanethi. 

Ii-audiobooks 
Inqaku eliphambili: 
I-audiobook okanye incwadi yokuthetha kukurekhodwa kwencwadi okanye omnye umsebenzi ofundwa ngokuvakalayo. Ukufundwa kombhalo opheleleyo kuchazwa “njengokungafinyezwanga”, ngelixa ukufundwa kweenguqulelo ezimfutshane kusishwankathelo. 

Irediyo ethethwayo ibifumaneka ezikolweni nakwiilayibrari zikawonke-wonke kwaye kancinci kwiivenkile zomculo ukusukela ngeminyaka yoo-1930. Iialbham ezininzi zamazwi athethwayo zenziwa ngaphambi kwexesha lekhasethi, iicompact disc, kunye neaudio enokukhutshelwa, edla ngokuba yimibongo nemidlalo kuneencwadi. Kwakungekho de kwangoo-1980 apho i-medium yaqala ukutsala abathengisi beencwadi, emva koko abathengisi beencwadi baqala ukubonisa ii-audiobooks kwiishelufa zeencwadi endaweni yokubonisa okwahlukileyo. 

Ebooks 
Inqaku eliphambili: I-Ebook 

A Kindle e-reader
I-ebook (ifutshane kwincwadi ye-elektroniki), nayo i-spelled e-book okanye i-eBook, yincwadi epapashiweyo eyenziwe ifumaneke ngohlobo lwe-elektroniki, equka umbhalo, imifanekiso, okanye zombini, efundeka kwi-flat panel display of computers or other electronic devices.[38] Nangona ngamanye amaxesha ichazwa "njengenguqulelo ye-elektroniki yencwadi eprintiweyo",[39] ezinye iincwadi ze-ebook zikhona ngaphandle kokuprintwa okufanayo. Ii-ebooks zinokufundwa kwizixhobo ezizinikezeleyo zokufunda i-e-reader nakuso nasiphi na isixhobo sekhompyuter esinesikrini esilawulekayo sokujonga, kubandakanya iikhompyuter zedesktop, iilaptops, iitafile kunye nee-smartphones. 

Kwezinye iimarike, ukuthengiswa kweencwadi ezishicilelweyo kwehlile ngenxa yokwanda kokusetyenziswa kwe-ebooks. Nangona kunjalo, iincwadi ezishicilelweyo zisathengiswa kakhulu kwii-ebooks, kwaye abantu abaninzi banomdla wokuprinta.[40][41][42][43] 

Iincwadi zemidiza 

Ukuthutyeleziswa komdiza ngencwadi 
Iincwadi zeDummy (okanye iincwadi zobuxoki) ziincwadi ezenzelwe ukuxelisa incwadi yokwenyani ngenkangeleko ukuze ziqhathe abantu, ezinye iincwadi zinokuba ziphelele zinamaphepha angenanto, ezinye zisenokuba zingenanto okanye kwezinye iimeko, kusenokubakho ipaneli epheleleyo eqingqwe ngemiqolo ethi emva koko ipeyintwe ukuze ibukeke njengeencwadi, izihloko zezinye iincwadi zisenokuba yintsomi. 

Kukho izizathu ezininzi zokuba neencwadi ze-dummy eziboniswe njenge; ukubalasela abatyeleli ngobutyebi obuninzi bolwazi abanalo kunye nokunyusa inkangeleko yomniniyo yobutyebi, ukufihla okuthile,[44] kwimiboniso yevenkile okanye ngeenjongo zokuhombisa. 

Ekuqaleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 eGwrych Castle, kuMntla Wales, uLloyd Hesketh Bamford-Hesketh wayesaziwa ngengqokelela yakhe enkulu yeencwadi kwithala lakhe, nangona kunjalo, ekupheleni kwaloo nkulungwane inye, uluntu lwaqaphela ukuba iinxalenye zethala leencwadi lakhe zaziyilweyile, iincwadi ezifihlakeleyo zazakhiwe zaza zatshixwa emva kweengcango zeglasi ukunqanda abantu ukuba bazame ukufikelela kuzo, ngokusuka kulo mzekeliso wethala leencwadi. ngaphandle".[45][46] 

Umxholo 

Eli candelo lifuna ucaphulo olongezelelweyo lokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Februwari 2024) (Funda ukuba ungawususa njani kwaye nini lo myalezo) 

Iinoveli ezikwivenkile ethengisa iincwadi 
Amathala eencwadi, iivenkile zeencwadi, kunye neengqokelela zidla ngokwahlulahlula iincwadi zibe yintsomi nezingezontsomi, nangona kukho ezinye iindidi ezingaphaya koku. Ezinye iincwadi, ezihlala zingapapashwanga okanye zipapashwe ngokuyintloko njengenxalenye yemisebenzi eyahlukeneyo yezoshishino (ezifana nezalathiso zeefowuni) azinakuthengiswa ngoovimba beencwadi okanye ziqokelelwe ngamathala eencwadi. Imibhalo-ngqangi, ii-logbooks kunye nezinye iirekhodi zinokuhlelwa kwaye zigcinwe ngokwahlukileyo ngeengqokelela ezikhethekileyo okanye oovimba. Iincwadi 

zeFiction 
Fiction ziqulethe imathiriyeli eyiliweyo, amabali aqhelekileyo. Ezinye iintlobo zoncwadi ezifana nesihobe zibandakanyiwe kudidi olubanzi. Uninzi lwamabali amabali angeyonyani luhlelwa ngokwemo yoncwadi kunye nohlobo.
 
Inoveli yeyona ndlela ixhaphakileyo yencwadi yefiction. Iinoveli yimisebenzi eyandisiweyo yebali eliyintsomi, ebonisa umxholo, umxholo, kunye nabalinganiswa. Le noveli ibe nefuthe elikhulu kwezolonwabo kunye nopapasho lwentengiso.[47][umthombo ongcono ofunekayo] I-novella ligama ngamanye amaxesha elisetyenziswa kwiprozi yentsomi ngokuqhelekileyo phakathi kwamagama angama-17,500 nama-40,000, kunye novelette phakathi kwama-7,500 nama-17,500. Ibali elifutshane linokuba nabuphi na ubude ukuya kutsho kumagama ali-10,000, kodwa la magama ubude ayahluka. 

Iincwadi ezihlekisayo okanye iinoveli zegraphic ziincwadi apho ibali lizotyiweyo. Abalinganiswa nababalisi basebenzisa amaqamza entetho okanye eengcinga ukuvakalisa ulwimi lomlomo. 

Ayiyonyani 

Iphepha elivela kwisichazi -magama
Iincwadi ezingezizo ezenyani zisekelwe kwinyani, eziquka izifundo ezifana nembali, ezopolitiko, imiba yezentlalo nenkcubeko, kunye neembali eziziibhayobhayom kunye neembali. Phantse lonke uncwadi lwezifundo aziyonyani. 

IiReferensi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Umsebenzi weereferensi 
Iincwadi ezineembekiselo ziincwadi ezingezizo ezenyani ekujoliswe kuzo ngokukhawuleza ekubhekiselwe kuzo ngolwazi, endaweni yokuba zifundwe ekuqaleni ukuya ekugqibeleni. Isimbo sokubhala esisetyenziswe kule misebenzi sinolwazi; ababhali bayaziphepha iimbono kunye nokusetyenziswa komntu wokuqala, kwaye bagxininise iinyani. 

Ialmanaka yincwadi yereferensi eqhelekileyo kakhulu, idla ngokuba ngumqulu omnye, enoluhlu lwedatha kunye nolwazi kwizihloko ezininzi. I-encyclopedia yincwadi okanye iseti yeencwadi ezenzelwe ukuba zibe namanqaku anzulu kwizihloko ezininzi. Incwadi edwelisa amagama, imvelaphi yawo, iintsingiselo zawo, nolunye ulwazi kuthiwa sisichazi-magama. Iatlasi yincwadi equlethe ingqokelela yeemephu. Incwadi yereferensi ekhethekileyo enika ulwazi malunga necandelo okanye ubuchule obuthile, obuhlala bujoliswe ekusetyenzisweni kobungcali, budla ngokubizwa ngokuba yincwadi yesandla. Iincwadi ezizama ukudwelisa iimbekiselo kunye nezicatshulwa kwindawo ethile ebanzi zinokubizwa ngokuba sisalathiso, njengeSalathiso soBunjineli, okanye izicatshulwa ezinjengeekhemikhali kunye nebhayoloji abstracts. 

Ubugcisa 
Bona kwakhona: Ukubhala ngobuchule Iincwadi 

zeatlasi 
ezinolwazi lobugcisa ngendlela yokwenza into ethile okanye indlela yokusebenzisa ezinye izixhobo zibizwa ngokuba ziincwadana zemiyalelo. Ezinye iincwadi ezithandwayo zibandakanya iincwadi zokupheka kunye neencwadi zokuphucula ikhaya. Abafundi 

bezeMfundo 
bahlala bephatha iincwadi zesikhokelo kunye neencwadi zesikolo ngeenjongo zokufunda. Iincwadi zeLap sisixhobo sokufunda esenziwe ngabafundi. Abafundi besikolo samabanga aphantsi basoloko besebenzisa iincwadi zokusebenza, ezipapashwa zinezithuba okanye izikhewu ukuze zizaliswe ngabo xa befunda okanye benze umsebenzi wesikolo owenzelwa ekhaya. Kwimfundo ephakamileyo yaseUnited States, kuyinto eqhelekileyo ukuba umfundi abhale iimviwo esebenzisa incwadi eluhlaza. Imibhalo 

yeNkolo  
: Isicatshulwa sezenkolo
, kubandakanywa nezibhalo, zizicatshulwa iinkolo ezahlukeneyo ezizithatha njengezona zibalulekileyo kwizithethe zabo zonqulo. Adla ngokuba nengqokelela okanye ingxubusho yeenkolelo, izithethe, imiyalelo nemithetho yokuziphatha, ukuziphatha okuhle, ulangazelelo lokomoya, nezibongozo zokukhuthaza ibutho lonqulo. 

Amaculo ziincwadi ezinengqokelela yamaculo omculo anokufumaneka rhoqo ezicaweni. Iincwadi zemithandazo okanye imijukujelwa ziincwadi ezinemithandazo ebhaliweyo yaye zidla ngokuphathwa ziimonki, oonongendi nabanye abalandeli abazinikeleyo okanye abefundisi. 

Iincwadi zabantwana 
Eli candelo licatshulwe kuncwadi lwaBantwana.[ hlela ] 

Umama ufundela abantwana bakhe phakathi ukuya ekupheleni kwenkulungwane ye-19 yelithograph nguJessie Willcox Smith.
Uncwadi lwabantwana okanye uncwadi lwabaselula lubandakanya amabali, iincwadi, iimagazini kunye nemibongo eyilelwe abantwana. Ukongeza kwiindidi zoncwadi eziqhelekileyo, uncwadi lwabantwana lwangoku luhlelwa ngokweminyaka ekujoliswe kuyo yomfundi, ukusuka kwiincwadi zemifanekiso zabaselula kakhulu ukuya kutsho kwiintsomi zabantu abadala abancinci kwabo basondela ekuvuthweni. 

Uncwadi lwabantwana lunokulandelwa kumabali emveli afana neentsomi, ezichongwe kuphela njengoncwadi lwabantwana ukususela kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesibhozo, kunye neengoma, eziyinxalenye yesithethe somlomo esibanzi, apho abantu abadala babebelana nabantwana ngaphambi kokuba bapapashe. Ukuphuhliswa koncwadi lwabantwana bokuqala, ngaphambi kokuba kuqalwe ukuprintwa, kunzima ukukulandelela. Kwanasemva kokuba ukuprintwa kuxhaphake, iintsomi ezininzi "zabantwana" zenzelwe abantu abadala kwaye kamva zilungelelaniselwe abaphulaphuli abancinci. Ukususela kwinkulungwane yeshumi elinesihlanu uncwadi oluninzi luye lwajoliswa ngokukodwa ebantwaneni, ngokufuthi lunomyalezo wokuziphatha okanye wenkolo. Uncwadi lwabantwana luye lwabunjwa yimithombo yonqulo, njengezithethe zamaPuritan, okanye ngeembono zentanda-bulumko nezenzululwazi ngeempembelelo zikaCharles Darwin noJohn Locke.[48] Ngasekupheleni kwenkulungwane yeshumi elinesithoba kunye nasekuqaleni kwenkulungwane yamashumi amabini zaziwa njenge "Golden Age of Children's Literature" kuba iincwadi ezininzi zabantwana zakudala zapapashwa ngoko. 

Iphepha elisuka kwincwadi yamanqaku esetyenziswa njengedayari ebhalwe ngesandla 
Engapapashwanga 
Jonga kwakhona: Uluhlu lweencwadi ezingapapashwanga 
Iincwadi ezininzi zisetyenziselwa kuphela ukurekhoda izimvo zobuqu, amanqaku, nee-akhawunti, ezinjengeencwadana zamanqaku, iincwadi zelogi, iincwadi eziqhelekileyo, kunye needayari. Ezi ncwadi azifane zipapashwe kwaye zidla ngokutshatyalaliswa okanye zihlale ziyimfihlo. 

Iincwadi zeedilesi, iincwadi zefowuni, kunye nekhalenda/iincwadi zokuqeshwa ziqhele ukusetyenziselwa ukurekhoda amadinga, iintlanganiso kunye nolwazi loqhagamshelwano lomntu. Amashishini ngokwembali ayesebenzisa iincwadi ze-accounting ezifana neejenali kunye neeledgers ukurekhoda idatha yezemali kwindlela ebizwa ngokuba yi-bookkeeping (ngoku edla ngokubanjelwa kwiikhomputha kunokuba ibhalwe ngesandla). 

Ukuqokelelwa kunye nokuhlelwa 

Eli candelo lifuna izicatshulwa ezongezelelweyo zokuqinisekisa. Nceda uncede ukuphucula eli nqaku ngokongeza izicatshulwa kwimithombo ethembekileyo kweli candelo. Izixhobo ezingasetyenziswanga zinokucelwa umngeni kwaye zisuswe. (Agasti 2024) (Funda indlela kwaye nini ukususa lo myalezo) 
Amathala eencwadi omntu kunye nawoluntu, oovimba kunye nezinye iindlela zokuqokelela iincwadi ziye zakhokelela ekudalweni kwemibutho emininzi eyahlukeneyo kunye nezicwangciso zokuhlela. Kwinkulungwane ye-19 neye-20, amathala eencwadi kunye neengcali zamathala eencwadi alungelelanise ukuqokelela iincwadi kunye neenkqubo zokuhlela ukuphendula kushishino olukhulayo. Eyona nkqubo isetyenziswa kakhulu yi-ISBN, ebonelele ngeempawu ezizodwa zeencwadi ukusukela ngo-1970. 

Amathala eencwadi 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ithala leencwadi

IThala leencwadi likaCelsus elise-Efese, eTurkey, lakhiwa ngo-135 AD, kwaye lalinokugcina imisongo emalunga ne-12,000. 
Ithala leencwadi yingqokelela yeencwadi, mhlawumbi nezinye izixhobo namajelo eendaba, anokufikelelwa ukuze asetyenziswe ngamalungu alo kunye namalungu amaziko amanyeneyo. Amathala eencwadi abonelela ngezinto eziphathekayo (iikopi ezingamaphepha) okanye zedijithali (iikopi ezithambileyo), kwaye inokuba yindawo ebonakalayo, indawo ebonakalayo, okanye zombini. Ingqokelela yethala leencwadi idla ngokubandakanya imathiriyeli eshicilelweyo enokubolekwa, kwaye ngokuqhelekileyo ikwabandakanya icandelo lereferensi yopapasho olunokusetyenziswa kuphela ngaphakathi kwizakhiwo. Izixhobo ezinjengokukhutshwa kweefilim, iinkqubo zikamabonakude, ezinye iividiyo ezirekhodiweyo, unomathotholo, umculo kunye noshicilelo lweaudio zinokufumaneka kwiifomathi ezininzi. Ezi ziquka iiDVD, iiBlu-rays, iiCD, iikhasethi, okanye ezinye iifomathi ezisebenzayo ezifana ne-microform. Basenokunikezela ngokufikelela kulwazi, umculo okanye omnye umxholo ogcinwe koovimba beenkcukacha zebhayibhilografi. 

Amathala eencwadi anokwahluka kakhulu ngobukhulu yaye anokulungiswa aze agcinwe liqumrhu likarhulumente elinjengorhulumente, iziko (elifana nesikolo okanye imyuziyam), iqumrhu, okanye umntu wabucala. Ukongeza ekuboneleleni ngemathiriyeli, amathala eencwadi akwabonelela ngeenkonzo zoonolayibrari abaqeqeshelwe ukufumana, ukukhetha, ukujikeleza nokulungelelanisa ulwazi ngelixa betolika iimfuno zolwazi kunye nokukhangela kunye nokuhlalutya izixa ezikhulu zolwazi ngezixhobo ezahlukeneyo. 

Izakhiwo zamathala eencwadi zidla ngokuba neendawo ezolileyo zokufundela, kwaneendawo eziqhelekileyo zokufundisisa neqela kunye nentsebenziswano, yaye zisenokubonelela ngeendawo zikawonke-wonke zokufikelela kwimithombo yazo ye-elektroniki, njengeekhompyutha nokufikelela kwi-Intanethi. 

Abathengi bethala leencwadi kunye neenkonzo ngokubanzi ezibonelelwayo ziyohluka ngokuxhomekeke kuhlobo lwayo: abasebenzisi bethala leencwadi loluntu banezidingo ezahlukileyo kwezo zethala leencwadi elikhethekileyo okanye ithala lemfundo, umzekelo. Amathala eencwadi asenokuba ziindawo zokuhlala, apho iinkqubo zenziwa zifumaneke kwaye abantu bazibandakanye kwimfundo yobomi bonke. Amathala eencwadi anamhlanje andisa iinkonzo zawo ngaphaya kweendonga ezibonakalayo zesakhiwo ngokubonelela ngemathiriyeli enokufikeleleka ngeendlela zombane, kuquka nasekhaya nge-Intanethi. 

Ukuchongwa kunye nokuhlelwa kwe 

-ISBN ngebhakhowudi
Ngo-2011, iManyano yaMazwe ngaMazwe yeMibutho yaMathala eeNcwadi kunye namaZiko (IFLA) yenza iNgcaciso yoMgangatho weBhayibhilografi yaMazwe ngaMazwe (ISBD) ukuze ilungelelanise iinkcazo kwiincwadi zeencwadi nakwiikhathalogu zamathala eencwadi. Incwadi nganye icaciswa yiNombolo yeNcwadi eMigangatho yaMazwe ngaMazwe, okanye i-ISBN, eyenzelwe ukuba yodwa kulo lonke uhlelo lwencwadi nganye eveliswa ngabapapashi abathatha inxaxheba, kwihlabathi jikelele. Ilawulwa yi-ISBN Society. I-ISBN ineenxalenye ezine: inxalenye yokuqala yikhowudi yelizwe, eyesibini ikhowudi yomshicileli, kunye neyesithathu ikhowudi yesihloko. Inxalenye yokugqibela yidijithi yokutshekisha, kwaye inokuthatha amaxabiso ukusuka ku-0–9 no-X (10). Iinombolo ze-EAN Barcodes zeencwadi zithathwe kwi-ISBN ngokufaka isimaphambili 978, kwi-Bookland, kunye nokubala idijithi yokutshekisha entsha. 

Abapapashi borhwebo kumazwe ahambele phambili kwezoshishino badla ngokunika ii-ISBNs ezincwadini zabo, ngoko ke abathengi banokucinga ukuba i-ISBN yinxalenye yenkqubo yamazwe ngamazwe iyonke, ngaphandle kwemikhethe. Nangona kunjalo, abapapashi bakarhulumente abaninzi, kumazwe amashishini kunye nasakhulayo, abathabathi nxaxheba ngokupheleleyo kwinkqubo ye-ISBN, kwaye bapapashe iincwadi ezingenazo ii-ISBN. Ingqokelela enkulu okanye yoluntu ifuna ikhathalogu. Iikhowudi ezibizwa ngokuba zii-"call numbers" zinxulumanisa iincwadi nekhathalogu, kwaye zimisele iindawo ezikuzo ezishelufini. Iinombolo zokufowuna zisekelwe kwinkqubo yokuhlelwa kweThala leeNcwadi. Inombolo yomnxeba ibekwe kumqolo wencwadi, ngokuqhelekileyo umgama omfutshane ngaphambi kwezantsi, nangaphakathi. Imigangatho yeziko okanye yesizwe, efana ne-ANSI/NISO Z39.41 – 1997, iseka indlela echanekileyo yokubeka ulwazi (njengesihloko, okanye igama lombhali) kwiincwadi ezijikelezayo, nakwizinto ezifana neencwadi “ezinoshelufa”, ezifana nezikhongozeli zeeDVD, iiteyiphu zevidiyo nesoftware. 


Iincwadi ezikwiishelufu zamathala eencwadi kunye neenombolo zokufowuna ezibonakala kwii- 
spines Enye inkqubo eyaziwa ngokubanzi yinkqubo yoHlelo lweThala leeNcwadi leCongress. Zombini ezi nkqubo zityekele kwizifundo ezazimelwe kakuhle kumathala eencwadi ase-US xa zaye zaphuhliswa, kwaye ngenxa yoko zineengxaki zokusingatha izifundo ezitsha, ezifana ne-computing, okanye izifundo ezinxulumene nezinye iinkcubeko.[49] Ulwazi malunga neencwadi kunye nababhali lunokugcinwa koovimba beenkcukacha ezifana noovimba beenkcukacha zeencwadi ezinomdla ngokubanzi kwi-intanethi. I-Metadata, ethetha "idatha malunga nedatha" lulwazi malunga nencwadi. Imethadatha malunga nencwadi inokubandakanya isihloko sayo, i-ISBN okanye enye inombolo yokuhlelwa (jonga ngasentla), amagama abaxhasi (umbhali, umhleli, umzobi) kunye nomshicileli, umhla kunye nobukhulu bayo, ulwimi lombhalo, umxholo wayo, njl.

Iinkqubo zokuhlela 
iBliss bibliographic classification (BC) 
Chinese Library Classification (CLC) 
Colon Classification 
Dewey Decimal Classification (DDC) 
iSkimu soHlelo olutsha lwamaThala eeNcwadi aseTshayina 
.
IThala leeNcwadi loHlelo lweNkongolo yeNkongolo (LCC) 
UHlelo lweDesimali oluqhelekileyo (UDC) 
ULondolozo 

Igcisa lolondolozo livavanya umsebenzi wobugcisa phantsi kwemakroskopu kwiMyuziyam yezoBugcisa yase-Indianapolis 
Ukugcinwa nokubuyiselwa kweencwadi, imibhalo-ngqangi, amaxwebhu, kunye ne-ephemera inikezelwe ekwandiseni ubomi bezinto zembali kunye nexabiso lobuqu elenziwe ngokuyintloko, ngesikhumba, ngesikhumba. Xa isetyenziswa kwilifa lenkcubeko, imisebenzi yolondolozo idla ngokuqhutywa ngumgcini. Eyona njongo iphambili yolondolozo kukwandisa ubomi bento kunye nokugcina ingqibelelo yayo ngokugcina zonke izongezo zibuyela umva. Ulondolozo lweencwadi kunye nephepha lubandakanya ubuchule bokudibanisa iincwadi, ukubuyisela, ukukhemikhali kwephepha, kunye nobunye ubugcisa bezinto eziphathekayo kuquka ugcino kunye nobuchule bokugcinwa koovimba.[50] 

Ugcino lwencwadi kunye nephepha lufuna ukuthintela kwaye, kwezinye iimeko, ukubuyisela umva umonakalo ngenxa yokuphatha, ubugwenxa bendalo, kunye nokusingqongileyo.[51][52] Abalondolozi bamisela iindlela ezifanelekileyo zokugcina iincwadi kunye namaxwebhu, kuquka iibhokisi kunye neshelufu ukuthintela umonakalo ongakumbi kunye nokukhuthaza ukugcinwa kwexesha elide.[53] Iindlela ezikhethwe ngononophelo kunye nobuchule bolondolozo olusebenzayo zinokubuyisela umva umonakalo kwaye zithintele umonakalo ongakumbi kwiibhetshi okanye unyango lwento enye esekelwe kwixabiso lencwadi okanye uxwebhu.[54] 

Ngokwembali, iindlela zokubuyisela iincwadi bezingekho ngokusesikweni kwaye ziqhutywa ziindima ezahlukeneyo kunye nemvelaphi yoqeqesho. Kule mihla, ukugcinwa kwamaxwebhu ephepha kunye neencwadi kaninzi kwenziwa ngumlondolozi oyingcali.[52][55] Abagcini bephepha okanye iincwadi ezininzi bangamalungu equmrhu leengcali, njengeAmerican Institute for Conservation (AIC) okanye iGuild of Bookworkers (zombini eUnited States), iArives and Records Association (eUnited Kingdom naseIreland), okanye iZiko loLondolozo (ICON) (eUnited Kingdom).[56] 

Imiba yezentlalo nenkcubeko 
Ulwamkelo 
Inqaku eliphambili: Ukugxekwa koncwadi 
Impembelelo yeencwadi inokuhluka, kwaye irekhodi yolwamkelo iza kwiifomathi ezininzi: ukuqala ngokwamkelwa koluntu okokuqala kumaphephandaba anamhlanje, inkcubeko yepop kunye nembalelwano, kwaye emva koko kuphuhliswe ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo zokugxekwa koncwadi ngabagxeki beengcali kunye nezemfundo. Kwishishini lokushicilela "uphononongo lwencwadi" yinxalenye ebalulekileyo yokwandisa ulwazi kunye nokwamkelwa kwencwadi: ekwaziyo ukwenza okanye ukwaphula uluvo loluntu malunga nencwadi entsha [icatshulwa] 

Uphononongo lwencwadi 
Eli candelo liyisicatshulwa kuphononongo lweNcwadi.[ hlela ] 
Uphononongo lwencwadi luhlobo lokugxekwa koncwadi apho incwadi ichazwa nje (uphononongo lwesishwankathelo) okanye ihlalutywe ngokusekelwe kumxholo, isimbo, kunye nesitayela, [5].

Uphononongo lwencwadi lunokuba ngumthombo ophambili, isicatshulwa soluvo, isishwankathelo sophononongo, okanye imbono yesifundiswa.[58] Iincwadi zinokujongwa kwakhona ukuze zishicilelwe kumaphepha-ndaba, amaphephancwadi namaphephandaba, njengomsebenzi wesikolo, okanye kwiiwebhusayithi zeencwadi kwi-Intanethi. Ubude bophononongo lwencwadi bunokwahluka ukusuka kumhlathi omnye ukuya kwisincoko esikhulu. Uhlolisiso olunjalo lunokuyihlolisisa le ncwadi ngokusekelwe kukhetho lobuqu. Ababuyekezi banokusebenzisa ithuba lophononongo lwencwadi kwisincoko esandisiweyo esinokuthi sisondelelene okanye sinxibelelene ngokusondeleyo nomxholo wencwadi, okanye ukwazisa izimvo zabo ngesihloko somsebenzi oyintsomi okanye ongeyonyani. 

Ezinye iijenali zinikezelwe kuphononongo lweencwadi, kwaye uphononongo lufakwe kwi-indexed database njenge-Book Review Index kunye noPhononongo lweKirkus; kodwa uphononongo lweencwadi ezininzi ngakumbi lunokufunyanwa kuluhlu lwedatha lwephephandaba kunye nolwezifundiswa olunjengoBugcisa noBuntu Citation Index, iSocial Sciences Citation Index, kunye noovimba beenkcukacha ezithe ngqo. 
Ukuhlolwa kweencwadi kunye nokuvalwa kweencwadi 
Ukuhlolwa kweencwadi sisenzo segunya elithile lithatha amanyathelo okucinezela iingcamango nolwazi olusencwadini.[59] Ulawulo "lulawulo lwentetho ekhululekileyo kunye nezinye iindlela zegunya elimiliselweyo".[60] Abahloli babona ngokuqhelekileyo njengomzali ochaphazelekayo, amalungu oluntu asabela kwisicatshulwa ngaphandle kokufunda, okanye imibutho yendawo okanye yesizwe.[61] Iincwadi ziye zahlolwa ngoozwilakhe abangoozwilakhe ukuze bavale umlomo abantu abaphikisayo, njengePeople's Republic of China, iJamani yamaNazi kunye neSoviet Union. Iincwadi zihlala zivavanyelwa ukufaneleka kweminyaka, ulwimi olukhubekisayo, umxholo wesondo, phakathi kwezinye izizathu.[62] Ngokufanayo, iinkolo zinokukhupha uluhlu lweencwadi ezivaliweyo, ezinjengomzekelo wembali we-Index yeCawa yamaKatolika, i-Librorum Prohibitorum kunye nokuvalwa kweencwadi ezifana nekaSalman Rushdie ethi The Satanic Verses ngu-Ayatollah Khomeini,[63] ezingasoloko ziphethe amandla asemthethweni. I-Censorship inokwenziwa kwinqanaba likazwelonke okanye le-subnational ngokunjalo, kwaye inokuthwala izohlwayo ezisemthethweni. Kwiimeko ezininzi, ababhali bezi ncwadi banokujamelana nezigwebo eziqatha, ukugxothwa kweli lizwe, okanye nokubulawa.[64][65] 

Ukutshiswa kwencwadi 
Eli candelo licatshulwe ekutshisweni kweNcwadi.[ hlela ] 

Ikopi yeNdlu yaMahlamvu iyatshiswa 
Ukutshiswa kwencwadi kukutshabalalisa ngabom ngomlilo weencwadi okanye ezinye izinto ezibhaliweyo, ezidla ngokuqhutywa kumxholo woluntu. Ukutshiswa kweencwadi kubonisa inkalo yokuvalwa kwaye ngokuqhelekileyo kuvela kwinkcaso yenkcubeko, yenkolo, okanye yezopolitiko kwizinto ekuthethwa ngazo.[66] Ukutshiswa kweencwadi kusenokuba sisenzo sokudelela okuqulethwe yincwadi okanye umbhali, okunenjongo yokutsalela ingqalelo yoluntu ngokubanzi kule nkcaso, okanye ukufihla inkcazelo equlethwe kwisicatshulwa ukuba ibhengezwe esidlangalaleni, njengeedayari okanye iileja. Ukutshisa kunye nezinye iindlela zokutshatyalaliswa kunye zaziwa ngokuba yi-biblioclasm okanye i-libricide.

Kwezinye iimeko, imisebenzi etshatyalalisiwe ayinakuphinda ibuyiselwe kwaye ukutshiswa kwayo kwenza ilahleko enkulu kwilifa lenkcubeko. Imizekelo ibandakanya ukutshiswa kweencwadi kunye nokungcwatywa kwabaphengululi phantsi kobukhosi baseTshayina baseQin (213-210 BCE), ukutshatyalaliswa kweNdlu yoBulumko ngexesha lokungqingwa kweMongol yaseBaghdad (1258), ukutshatyalaliswa kweekhowudi ze-Aztec ngu-Itzcoatl (1430s), ukutshiswa kwee-Maya codices 5 kunye ne-Landang 6 Diego kwi-Landang 6 de Diego (6) Jaffna Public Library e Sri Lanka (1981).[68] 

Kwezinye iimeko, ezinjengokutshiswa kweencwadi zamaNazi, imibhalo yeencwadi ezitshatyalalisiweyo iyasinda, kodwa ukutshiswa kweencwadi kuba ngumfuziselo wolawulo olungqwabalala nolucinezelayo olufuna ukuvalela okanye ukuvala inkalo ethile yenkcubeko ekhoyo.
